# <a name="hololens-2-release-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-103">HoloLens 2 版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-103">HoloLens 2 release notes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-104">為了確保您的 HoloLens 裝置有生產力的體驗，我們會繼續發行功能、bug 和安全性更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-104">To ensure you have a productive experience with your HoloLens devices, we continue to release feature, bug, and security updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-105">在此頁面上，您可以看到每個月 HoloLens 的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-105">On this page, you can see what’s new for HoloLens each month.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-106">若要取得最新的 HoloLens 2 更新，您可以[檢查是否有更新，並以手動方式更新](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update)或取得完整 Flash 更新， (FFU) 透過[Advanced Recovery 隨附將裝置閃爍](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-106">To get the latest HoloLens 2 update, you can either [check for updates and manually update](hololens-update-hololens.md#check-for-updates-and-manually-update) or get the Full Flash Update (FFU) to [flash your device via Advanced Recovery Companion](hololens-recovery.md#clean-reflash-the-device).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-107">[下載](https://aka.ms/hololens2download)會保持最新狀態，並提供最新正式推出的組建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-107">The [download](https://aka.ms/hololens2download) is kept up to date and provides the latest generally available build.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-108">最新的 Windows 11 公告著重于電腦版本的 Windows。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-108">The recent Windows 11 announcement was focused on the PC version of Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-109">我們最近在2021年5月推出了 HoloLens 2 的[重大作業系統更新](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067)，我們正努力根據客戶對此秋季的意見反應，來處理即將推出的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-109">We recently launched a [major OS update](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/mixed-reality-blog/what-s-new-in-windows-holographic-version-21h1/ba-p/2337067) to HoloLens 2 in May 2021, and we are working on an upcoming release based on customer feedback for this fall.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-110">由於[21H1 組建中已解決的已知問題會影響遠端協助使用者](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes)，我們暫時暫停了 Windows 全像版本21H1 更新的供應專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-110">Due to a now resolved [known issue in our 21H1 build that was affecting Remote Assist users](hololens-troubleshooting.md#remote-assist-video-freezes-after-20-minutes), we temporally paused the offering of Windows Holographic, version 21H1 updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-111">我們也已將預設的 Advanced Recovery 附隨 (ARC) 組建變更為 Windows 全像[20H2 版–2021年6月更新](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-111">We had also changed the default Advanced Recovery Companion (ARC) build to the [Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – June 2021 Update](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-112">ARC 組建現在會繼續以21H1 組建為目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-112">The ARC build will now resume targeting the 21H1 build.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1---june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-113">Windows全像21H1 版-2021 年6月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-113">Windows Holographic, version 21H1 - June 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-114">組建20348.1007</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-114">Build 20348.1007</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive-for-work-or-school-camera-roll-upload"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-115">適用于公司或學校相機的 OneDrive 滾動上傳</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-115">OneDrive for work or school Camera Roll upload</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-116">我們已將新功能新增至 HoloLens 2 設定應用程式，這可讓客戶從裝置的圖片自動上傳混合現實照片和影片 > 相機滾動資料夾到工作或學校資料夾的對應 OneDrive。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-116">We've added a new feature to the HoloLens 2 Settings app, which allows customers to automatically upload mixed reality photos and videos from the device's Pictures > Camera Roll folder to the corresponding OneDrive for work or school folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-117">這項功能可解決 HoloLens 2 上[OneDrive 應用程式內的功能缺口](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos)，而這項功能只支援將相機上傳至客戶的個人 Microsoft 帳戶 (，而非其公司或學校帳戶) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-117">This feature addresses a [feature gap within the OneDrive app](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#share-your-mixed-reality-photos-and-videos) on HoloLens 2, which only supports automatic Camera Roll upload to a customer's personal Microsoft account (and not their work or school account).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-118">**運作方式**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-118">**How it works**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-119">造訪 **設定 > 系統 > 混合實境相機**，以啟用「相機上傳」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-119">Visit **Settings > System > Mixed Reality Camera** to enable "Camera upload."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-120">藉由將這項功能設定為 [**開啟**] 位置，將會自動將任何與您的裝置相關的混合現實照片或影片上傳至您 OneDrive for work 或學校帳戶的 [圖片] > 相機滾動資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-120">By setting this feature to the **On** position, any mixed reality photos or videos captured to your device will automatically be queued for upload to the Pictures > Camera Roll folder of your OneDrive for work or school account.</span></span>
    >[!NOTE]
    ><span data-ttu-id="8175b-121">在啟用這項功能之前所捕獲到的相片和影片， *將不* 會排入上傳佇列，也將需要手動上傳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-121">Photos and videos captured prior to enabling this feature *will not* be queued for upload and will still need to be manually uploaded.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-122">在 [設定] 頁面上的狀態訊息將會顯示 [正在等待上傳的檔案數目] (或 [OneDrive 是最新狀態]，以) 上傳所有暫止的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-122">A status message on the Settings page will display the number of files pending upload (or read "OneDrive is up to date" when all pending files have been uploaded).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-123">如果您擔心頻寬，或是基於任何原因而想要「暫停」上傳，您可以將功能切換到 **Off** 位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-123">If you're concerned about bandwidth or want to "pause" upload for any reason, you can switch the feature to the **Off** position.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-124">暫時停用此功能，可確保當您將新檔案新增至相機暫存資料夾時，上傳佇列會繼續增加，但在您重新啟用功能之前，將不會上傳檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-124">Temporarily disabling the feature ensures that the upload queue will continue to increase as you add new files to the Camera Roll folder, but files will not upload until you re-enable the feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-125">最新的檔案會先上傳 (最後一個) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-125">Newest files will upload first (last in, first out).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-126">如果您的 OneDrive 帳戶有問題 (例如，您的密碼變更之後) [**立即修正**] 按鈕將會出現在 [設定] 頁面上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-126">If your OneDrive account has issues (for example, after your password changes) a **Fix now** button will appear on the Settings page.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-127">檔案大小沒有上限，但請注意，大型檔案需要較長的時間才能上傳 (特別是當您的上傳頻寬受限於) 時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-127">There is no maximum file size, but note that large files will take longer to upload (especially if your upload bandwidth is constrained).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-128">如果您在上傳大型檔案時「暫停」或關閉上傳，則會保留部分上傳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-128">If you "pause" or turn off upload while a large file is being uploaded, the partial upload will be preserved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-129">如果上傳在數小時內被「暫停」或「關閉」，則上傳會從中斷的位置繼續進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-129">If upload is re-enabled within several hours of being "paused" or turned off, the upload will continue from where it left off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-130">但是，如果在數小時後重新啟用上傳，則會從頭開始重新開機大型檔案的上傳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-130">However, if upload is re-enabled after several hours, the large file's upload will restart from the beginning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-131">**已知問題和警告**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-131">**Known issues and caveats**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-132">這項設定不會根據目前的頻寬使用量進行內建的節流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-132">This setting has no built in throttling based on current bandwidth usage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-133">如果您需要將其他案例的頻寬最大化，請手動關閉設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-133">If you need to maximize bandwidth for another scenario, turn off the setting manually.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-134">Upload 將會暫停，但功能會繼續監視新增至攝影機的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-134">Upload will be paused but the feature will continue to monitor newly added files to Camera Roll.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-135">當您準備好要繼續進行上傳時，請重新啟用上傳。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-135">Re-enable upload when you're ready for it to continue.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-136">您必須針對裝置上的每個使用者帳戶啟用這項功能，而且只能主動上傳目前登入裝置之使用者的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-136">This feature must be enabled for each user account on the device, and it can only actively upload files for the user who is currently signed-in to the device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-137">如果您在觀看設定頁面上的上傳計數時拍攝相片或影片，請注意，在目前的檔案完成上傳之前，暫止的檔案計數可能不會變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-137">If you're taking photos or videos while watching the upload count on the Settings page in real-time, note that the pending file count may not change until the current file has completed uploading.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-138">如果您的裝置處於睡眠或關閉電源，Upload 將會暫停。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-138">Upload will pause if your device falls asleep or is powered off.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-139">若要確保您的暫止上傳完成，請主動使用裝置，直到設定頁面閱讀「OneDrive 為最新狀態」或調整您的 **電源 & 睡眠** 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-139">To ensure your pending uploads complete, actively use the device until the Settings page reads "OneDrive is up to date" or adjust your **Power & sleep** settings.</span></span>
### <a name="added-support-for-some-telemetry-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-140">已新增某些遙測原則的支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-140">Added support for some telemetry policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-141">HoloLens 2 現在支援下列遙測原則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-141">The following telemetry policies are now supported on the HoloLens 2:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-142">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-142">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-143">DisableDeviceDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-143">DisableDeviceDelete</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-144">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-144">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-145">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-145">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-146">System\AllowTelemetry 和 System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx 都應該一起使用，以在設定應用程式中擁有遙測和行為的完整控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-146">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-147">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-147">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-148">使用色彩校正來修正主要的視頻損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-148">Fixes major video corruption with Color calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-149">解決可能會在 [電源] 功能表中截斷文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-149">Addresses an issue where text might be truncated in the Power menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-150">啟用 RequirePrivateStoreOnly 原則的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-150">Enables support for the RequirePrivateStoreOnly policy.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2--june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-151">Windows全像版本20H2 –2021年6月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-151">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – June 2021 Update</span></span>

### <a name="added-support-for-some-telemetry-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-153">已新增某些遙測原則的支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-153">Added support for some telemetry policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-154">HoloLens 2 現在支援下列遙測原則：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-154">The following telemetry policies are now supported on the HoloLens 2:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-155">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-155">ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-156">DisableDeviceDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-156">DisableDeviceDelete</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-157">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-157">AllowDeviceNameInDiagnosticData</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-158">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-158">FeedbackHubAlwaysSaveDiagnosticsLocally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-159">System\AllowTelemetry 和 System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx 都應該一起使用，以在設定應用程式中擁有遙測和行為的完整控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-159">Both System\AllowTelemetry and System\ConfigureTelemetryOptInSettingsUx should be used together to have complete control on the Telemetry and behavior in the Settings app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-160">我們建議您試用最新的組建，Windows 全像21H1 版。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-160">We encourage you to try out our latest build, Windows Holographic, version 21H1.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---june-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-161">Windows全像1903版-2021 年6月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-161">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - June 2021 Update</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-163">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-163">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-165">此組建將不再提供服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-165">This build will no longer be serviced.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-21h1"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-166">Windows全像21H1 版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-166">Windows Holographic, version 21H1</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-167">組建20346.1002</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-167">Build 20346.1002</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-168">此更新包含兩個目標使用者的功能;使用者可由裝置上的任何人使用的功能，以及可由 IT 系統管理員設定的新裝置管理選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-168">This update contains features for two target audiences; features that can be used by anyone on a device by the End User, and new device management options that can be configured by IT Admins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-169">下表指定與每個物件相關的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-169">The table below specifies the features that are relevant to each audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-170">如果您是 IT 系統管理員，請看看我們的 [It 系統管理員-更新檢查清單](#it-admin---update-checklist)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-170">If you are an IT Admin, please take a look at our [IT Admin - Update Checklist](#it-admin---update-checklist).</span></span>
>[!IMPORTANT]
><span data-ttu-id="8175b-171">若要更新為此組建，HoloLens 2 裝置 (s) 必須目前正在執行2021年2月更新 (組建 19041.1136) 或更新版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-171">In order to update to this build, HoloLens 2 device(s) must be currently running the February 2021 update (build 19041.1136) or newer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-172">如果您未看到此功能更新可供使用，請先更新您的裝置，然後再試一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-172">If you are not seeing this feature update available, please update your device first and try again.</span></span>

>[!NOTE]
><span data-ttu-id="8175b-173">目前，Microsoft HoloLens 2 支援 (錯誤和安全性修正的每月服務更新) 適用于下列版本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-173">Today, Microsoft HoloLens 2 supports monthly servicing updates (bug and security fixes) for the following releases:</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-174">Windows全像20H2 版 (Build 19041.1128 +) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-174">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 (Build 19041.1128+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-175">Windows全像2004版 (Build 19041.1103 +) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-175">Windows Holographic, version 2004 (Build 19041.1103+)</span></span>
>- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-176">Windows全像1903版 (Build 18362 +) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-176">Windows Holographic, version 1903 (Build 18362+)</span></span> 
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-177">隨著 Windows 的全像21H1 版，**我們會停止全像1903版的每月服務 Windows 更新**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-177">With the introduction of Windows Holographic version 21H1, **we are discontinuing monthly servicing updates for Windows Holographic version 1903**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-178">這可讓我們專注于較新的版本，並持續提供重要的改良功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-178">This enables us to focus on more recent releases and continue to deliver valuable improvements.</span></span>

### <a name="introducing-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-243">新 Microsoft Edge 簡介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-243">Introducing the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

![舊版 Microsoft Edge 標誌至新 Microsoft Edge 標誌的動畫](images/new-edge.gif)

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-245">新的 Microsoft Edge[採用 Chromium 的開放原始碼專案](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/)，為客戶建立更好的相容性，並為 網頁程式開發人員提供較少的 web 片段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-245">The new Microsoft Edge [adopts the Chromium open source project](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2018/12/06/microsoft-edge-making-the-web-better-through-more-open-source-collaboration/) to create better compatibility for customers and less fragmentation of the web for web developers.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-246">這個新的 Microsoft Edge 會自動取代新版本不再[支援](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/)的舊版 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-246">This new Microsoft Edge automatically replaces legacy Microsoft Edge, which is [no longer supported](https://blogs.windows.com/msedgedev/2021/03/09/microsoft-edge-legacy-end-of-support/) in new releases.</span></span>

![新的 Microsoft Edge 螢幕擷取畫面](images/new-edge-ui.png)

#### <a name="launching-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-248">啟動新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-248">Launching the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-249">新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-249">The new Microsoft Edge</span></span> ![新增 Microsoft Edge 圖示](images/new_edge_logo.png) <span data-ttu-id="8175b-251">以藍色和綠色的紋圖示表示的 () 會釘選到 [開始] 功能表，並且會在您啟用 web 連結時自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-251">(represented by a blue and green swirl icon) is pinned to the Start menu and will automatically launch when you activate a web link.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-252">當您第一次在 HoloLens 2 上啟動新的 Microsoft Edge 時，將會從舊版 Microsoft Edge 匯入您的設定和資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-252">When you first launch the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2, your settings and data will be imported from legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-253">如果您在啟動新的 Microsoft Edge 之後繼續使用舊版 Microsoft Edge，新的資料將不會從舊版 Microsoft Edge 同步至新的 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-253">If you continue to use legacy Microsoft Edge after launching the new Microsoft Edge, that new data will not be synced from legacy Microsoft Edge to the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

#### <a name="configuring-policy-settings-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-254">正在設定新 Microsoft Edge 的原則設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-254">Configuring policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-255">新的 Microsoft Edge 為 IT 系統管理員提供比先前舊版 Microsoft Edge 更廣泛的瀏覽器原則組 HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-255">The new Microsoft Edge offers IT admins a much broader set of browser policies on HoloLens 2 than were previously available with legacy Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-256">以下是一些實用的資源，可讓您深入瞭解如何管理新 Microsoft Edge 的原則設定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-256">Here are some helpful resources for learning more about managing policy settings for the new Microsoft Edge:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-257">使用 Microsoft Intune 設定 Microsoft Edge 原則設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-257">Configure Microsoft Edge policy settings with Microsoft Intune</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/configure-edge-with-intune)
- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-258">舊版 Microsoft Edge Microsoft Edge 原則對應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-258">Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)
- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-259">Google Chrome Microsoft Edge 原則對應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-259">Google Chrome to Microsoft Edge policy mapping</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-chrome-to-newedge)
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-260">完整[Microsoft Edge Enterprise 檔](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-260">Full [Microsoft Edge Enterprise documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/)</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-261">由於新 Microsoft Edge 支援的瀏覽器原則數量，我們的小組無法保證每個新原則都能在 HoloLens 2 上運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-261">Because of the volume of browser policies supported by the new Microsoft Edge, our team is unable to guarantee that each new policy works on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-262">不過，我們已經過測試並確認，與先前在 HoloLens 2 如預期般支援的每個舊版 Microsoft Edge 原則相等的新 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-262">However, we've tested and confirmed than the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge policy previously supported on HoloLens 2 work as expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-263">請參閱[舊版 Microsoft Edge Microsoft Edge 原則對應](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge)，以找出與 HoloLens 2 使用的每個舊版 Microsoft Edge 瀏覽器原則相等的新 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-263">See [Microsoft Edge Legacy to Microsoft Edge policy mapping](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-policy-map-legacy-to-newedge) to find the new Microsoft Edge equivalent of each legacy Microsoft Edge browser policy you were using with HoloLens 2.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-264">至少有兩個新的 Microsoft Edge 原則，我們知道 *將無法* 與 HoloLens 2 搭配使用：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-264">There are at least two new Microsoft Edge policies that we know *will not* work with HoloLens 2:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-265">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-265">EnterpriseModeSiteList</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-266">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-266">EnterpriseSiteListServiceURL</span></span>

#### <a name="what-to-expect-from-the-new-microsoft-edge-on-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-267">新 Microsoft Edge 在 HoloLens 2 的預期結果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-267">What to expect from the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-268">因為新的 Microsoft Edge 是原生的 Win32 應用程式，具有新的 uwp 介面卡層可讓它在僅限 UWP 的裝置上執行（例如 HoloLens 2），所以某些功能可能無法立即可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-268">Because the new Microsoft Edge is a native Win32 app with a new UWP adapter layer allowing it to run on UWP-only devices like HoloLens 2, some features may not be immediately available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-269">我們將在未來幾個月內支援新的案例和功能，因此請查看此空間以取得最新資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-269">We'll be supporting new scenarios and features over the coming months, so check this space for up-to-date information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-270">**預期運作的案例和功能：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-270">**Scenarios and features expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-271">首次執行體驗，登入以進行分析，並進行同步處理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-271">First-run experience, sign in to profile, and sync</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-272">網站應該會如預期般呈現和行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-272">Websites should render and behave as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-273">大部分的瀏覽器功能 (我的最愛、歷程記錄等 ) 應能如預期般運作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-273">Most browser functionality (Favorites, History, etc.) should work as expected</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-274">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-274">Dark mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-275">將 web 應用程式安裝至裝置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-275">Installing web apps to the device</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-276">安裝延伸模組 (請讓我們知道您是否使用任何無法在 HoloLens 2 上正常運作的延伸模組) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-276">Installing extensions (please let us know if you use any extensions that don't work properly on HoloLens 2)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-277">觀賞和標記 PDF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-277">Viewing and marking up a PDF</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-278">從單一瀏覽器視窗的空間音效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-278">Spatial sound from a single browser window</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-279">瀏覽器的自動和手動更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-279">Automatic and manual updating of the browser</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-280">使用 [儲存至 PDF] 選項，從 [列印] 功能表 (儲存 PDF) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-280">Saving a PDF from the Print menu (using "Save to PDF" option)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-281">WebXR 和360檢視器擴充功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-281">WebXR and 360 Viewer extension</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-282">當您在環境中的多個視窗之間流覽時，內容還原至正確的視窗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-282">Content restoration to correct window, when browsing across multiple windows placed in your environment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-283">**不應運作的案例和功能：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-283">**Scenarios and features not expected to work:**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-284">具有同時音訊串流的多個視窗的空間音效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-284">Spatial sound from multiple windows with simultaneous audio streams</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-285">「看它，說它」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-285">"See it, say it"</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-286">列印</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-286">Printing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-287">**最常見的瀏覽器已知問題：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-287">**Top browser known issues:**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-288">新的 Microsoft Edge 已停用全像鍵盤上的放大鏡預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-288">The magnifier preview in the holographic keyboard has been disabled for the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-289">建議您在未來的更新中重新啟用這項功能，一旦縮放比例正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-289">We hope to reenable this feature in a future update, once the magnification is working correctly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-290">如果您有另一個瀏覽器視窗開啟且作用中，則可能會從錯誤的瀏覽器視窗播放音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-290">Audio may play from the wrong browser window if you have another browser window open and active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-291">您可以藉由關閉不應該播放音訊的其他使用中視窗來解決此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-291">You can work around this issue by closing the other active window that isn't supposed to be playing audio.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-292">當您在「 [跟隨我」模式](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following)的瀏覽器視窗中播放音訊時，如果您停用「跟隨我」模式，音訊將繼續播放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-292">When playing audio from a browser window in ["Follow me" mode](hololens2-basic-usage.md#follow-me-stop-following), the audio will continue playing if you disable "Follow me" mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-293">若要解決此問題，您可以在停用「跟隨我」模式或使用 [ **X** ] 按鈕關閉視窗之前，先停止播放音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-293">You can work around this issue by stopping audio playback before disabling "Follow me" mode or by closing the window with the **X** button.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-294">與作用中的 Microsoft Edge windows 互動，可能會導致其他2d 應用程式視窗意外變成非使用中狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-294">Interacting with active Microsoft Edge windows may cause other 2D app windows to go inactive unexpectedly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-295">您可以重新開機這些視窗，方法是再次與其互動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-295">You can reactivate these windows by interacting with them again.</span></span>

#### <a name="microsoft-edge-insider-channels"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-296">Microsoft EdgeInsider 頻道</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-296">Microsoft Edge Insider channels</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-297">Microsoft Edge 團隊提供三個預覽頻道給 Edge Insider 車隊：搶鮮版（Beta）、開發和的測試。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-297">The Microsoft Edge team makes three preview channels available to the Edge Insider community: Beta, Dev, and Canary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-298">安裝預覽通道不會卸載 HoloLens 2 上的 Microsoft Edge 發行版本，而且可以同時安裝一個以上的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-298">Installing a preview channel doesn't uninstall the released version of Microsoft Edge on your HoloLens 2, and you can install more than one at the same time.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-299">造訪[Microsoft Edge Insider 首頁](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com)，以深入瞭解 Edge 測試人員群體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-299">Visit the [Microsoft Edge Insider homepage](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com) to learn more about the Edge Insider community.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-300">若要深入瞭解不同的 Edge Insider 頻道並開始使用，請造訪 [Edge insider 下載頁面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-300">To learn more about the different Edge Insider channels and get started, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-301">有幾種方法可將 Microsoft Edge Insider 通道安裝到 HoloLens 2：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-301">There are a couple methods available for installing Microsoft Edge Insider channels to HoloLens 2:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-302">**裝置上的直接安裝 (目前僅適用于非受控裝置)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-302">**Direct install on device (currently only available to unmanaged devices)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-303">在您的 HoloLens 2 上，流覽[Edge Insider 下載頁面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-303">On your HoloLens 2, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-304">針對您想要安裝的 Edge Insider 頻道，請選取 [**下載] HoloLens 2** 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-304">Select the **Download for HoloLens 2** button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-305">使用檔案總管) ，從 Edge 下載佇列或裝置的 [下載] 資料夾 (啟動下載的 msix 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-305">Launch the downloaded .msix file from the Edge download queue or from your device's "Downloads" folder (using File Explorer).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-306">將會啟動[應用程式安裝程式](app-deploy-app-installer.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-306">[App installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md) will launch.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-307">選取 [安裝] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-307">Select the **Install** button.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-308">成功安裝之後，您會在 [開始] 功能表的 **所有應用程式** 清單中找到 Microsoft Edge Beta、開發或全像是個別專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-308">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-309">**透過具有 Windows 裝置入口網站的電腦安裝 (需要在 HoloLens 2 上啟用 [開發人員模式](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal))**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-309">**Install via PC with Windows Device Portal (requires [developer mode](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#setting-up-hololens-to-use-windows-device-portal) to be enabled on HoloLens 2)**</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-310">在您的電腦上，流覽 [Edge Insider 下載頁面](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-310">On your PC, visit the [Edge Insider download page](https://www.microsoftedgeinsider.com/download).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-311">針對您想要安裝的 Edge Insider 頻道，選取 [下載 Windows 10] 按鈕旁的 **下拉箭號按鈕**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-311">Select the **drop-down arrow button** next to the "Download for Windows 10" button for the Edge Insider channel you wish to install.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-312">在下拉式功能表中選取 **HoloLens 2** 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-312">Select **HoloLens 2** in the drop-down menu.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-313">將 msix 檔案儲存到您電腦的 [下載] 資料夾 (或您可以輕鬆找到) 的另一個資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-313">Save the .msix file to the "Downloads" folder of your PC (or another folder you can easily find).</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-314">在您的電腦上使用[Windows 裝置入口網站](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app)，在 HoloLens 2 上安裝下載的 msix 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-314">Use [Windows Device Portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/develop/platform-capabilities-and-apis/using-the-windows-device-portal#installing-an-app) on your PC to install the downloaded .msix file on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-315">成功安裝之後，您會在 [開始] 功能表的 **所有應用程式** 清單中找到 Microsoft Edge Beta、開發或全像是個別專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-315">After successful install, you'll find Microsoft Edge Beta, Dev, or Canary as a separate entry in the **All apps** list of the Start menu.</span></span>

#### <a name="using-wdac-to-block-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-316">使用 WDAC 封鎖新的 Microsoft Edge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-316">Using WDAC to block new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-317">如果 IT 系統管理員想要更新其[WDAC 原則](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md)以封鎖新的 Microsoft Edge 應用程式，您必須將下列程式新增至您的原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-317">For IT Admins looking to update their [WDAC policy](windows-defender-application-control-wdac.md) to block the new Microsoft Edge app, you'll need to add the following to your policy.</span></span>

``` <Deny ID="ID_DENY_D_3_0" FriendlyName="C:\Data\Programs FileRule" PackageVersion="65535.65535.65535.65535" FileName="msedge.exe" /> ```

#### <a name="managing-endpoints-for-the-new-microsoft-edge"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-318">管理新 Microsoft Edge 的端點</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-318">Managing endpoints for the new Microsoft Edge</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-319">某些環境可能會有網路限制，以考慮考慮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-319">Some environments may have network restrictions to account for as a consideration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-320">若要確保新的邊緣有順暢的體驗，請 [啟用這些 Microsoft 端點。](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-320">To ensure a smooth experience with the new Edge please [enable these Microsoft endpoints.](https://docs.microsoft.com/deployedge/microsoft-edge-security-endpoints)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-321">深入瞭解目前可用的[端點以進行 HoloLens](hololens-offline.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-321">Read more about the currently available [endpoints for HoloLens](hololens-offline.md).</span></span>

### <a name="install-web-apps"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-322">安裝 web apps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-322">Install web apps</span></span>
 > [!Note]
><span data-ttu-id="8175b-323">從 Windows 全像[21H1 版](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1)，Office web 應用程式將不再預先安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-323">As of [Windows Holographic, version 21H1](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-21h1), the Office web app will no longer be pre-installed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-324">您可以使用新的 Edge，將 web 應用程式與 Microsoft Store 應用程式一起安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-324">You can use the new Edge to install web apps alongside Microsoft Store apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-325">例如，您可以安裝 Microsoft Office web 應用程式，以查看及編輯裝載于 SharePoint 或 OneDrive 的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-325">For example, you can install the Microsoft Office web app to view and edit files hosted on SharePoint or OneDrive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-326">若要安裝 Office web 應用程式，請流覽 https://www.office.com 並選取網址列中的 **可用應用程式**，或 **安裝 Office** 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-326">To install the Office web app, visit https://www.office.com and select the **App Available** or **Install Office** button in the address bar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-327">選取 [ **安裝** ] 以確認。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-327">Select **Install** to confirm.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-328">只有當您的 HoloLens 2 具有作用中的網際網路連線時，才可使用 Office web 應用程式功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-328">Office web app functionality is only available when your HoloLens 2 has an active internet connection.</span></span>

### <a name="webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-329">WebXR 和360檢視器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-329">WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-330">新的 Microsoft Edge 包含 WebXR 的支援，這是建立沉浸式 web 體驗的新標準， (取代 WebVR) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-330">The new Microsoft Edge includes support for WebXR, which is the new standard for creating immersive web experiences (replacing WebVR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-331">許多沉浸式 web 體驗的設計都是以 VR 來設計 (它們會將您的觀點取代為虛擬環境) ，但 HoloLens 2 也支援這些體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-331">Many immersive web experiences were designed with VR in mind (they replace your field of view with a virtual environment), but these experiences are also supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-332">WebXR 標準也可提供使用您的實體環境的增強和混合現實的沉浸式 web 體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-332">The WebXR standard also enables augmented and mixed reality immersive web experiences that use your physical environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-333">當開發人員花更多時間 WebXR 時，我們預期新的增強和混合現實將可讓 HoloLens 2 客戶試用！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-333">As developers spend more time with WebXR, we anticipate new augmented and mixed reality immersive experiences will arrive for HoloLens 2 customers to try!</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-334">360檢視器延伸模組建置於 WebXR 上，並會隨著新的 Microsoft Edge 在 HoloLens 2 上自動安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-334">The 360 Viewer extension is built on WebXR and automatically installs alongside the new Microsoft Edge on HoloLens 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-335">此 web 擴充功能可讓您在360度的影片中自行 immerse。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-335">This web extension gives you the ability to immerse yourself in 360-degree videos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-336">YouTube 提供最大的360影片選擇，因此建議您從該處開始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-336">YouTube offers the largest selection of 360 videos, so we encourage you to start there.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use-webxr"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-337">如何使用 WebXR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-337">How to use WebXR</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-338">流覽至具有 WebXR 支援的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-338">Navigate to a website with WebXR support.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-339">選取網站上的 [ **輸入 VR** ] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-339">Select the **Enter VR** button on the website.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-340">此按鈕的位置和視覺標記法可能會因網站而異，但看起來可能類似：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-340">The location and visual representation of this button may vary per website, but it may look similar to:</span></span>

    ![輸入 VR 按鈕範例](images/75px-enter-vr.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-342">當您第一次嘗試在特定網域上啟動 WebXR 經驗時，瀏覽器會要求同意進入沉浸式觀賞，請選取 [ **允許**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-342">The first time you try to launch a WebXR experience on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view, select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-343">使用[HoloLens 2 手勢](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame)來操作體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-343">Use [HoloLens 2 gestures](hololens2-basic-usage.md#the-hand-tracking-frame) to manipulate the experience.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-344">如果體驗沒有 **結束按鈕，** 請使用 [開始手勢](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) 來返回 home。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-344">If the experience doesn't have an **Exit** button, use the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) to return home.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-345">**建議的 WebXR 範例**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-345">**Recommended WebXR samples**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-346">360檢視器 (請參閱下一節) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-346">360 Viewer (see next section)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-347">XR Dinosaurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-347">XR Dinosaurs</span></span>](https://www.xrdinosaurs.com/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-348">Barista Express</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-348">Barista Express</span></span>](https://constructarca.de/game/barista-express/)
- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-349">WebXR 小畫家</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-349">WebXR Paint</span></span>](https://threejs.org/examples/webxr_vr_paint.html)

#### <a name="how-to-use-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-350">如何使用360檢視器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-350">How to use 360 Viewer</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-351">流覽至 YouTube 上的360度影片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-351">Navigate to a 360-degree video on YouTube.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-352">在影片畫面中，選取 [混合現實耳機] 按鈕：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-352">In the video frame, select the mixed reality headset button:</span></span>

    ![啟用360檢視器的按鈕](images/enter-360-viewer.jpg)

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-354">當您第一次嘗試在特定網域上啟動360檢視器時，瀏覽器會要求同意進入沉浸式觀看。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-354">The first time you try to launch 360 Viewer on a specific domain, the browser will ask for consent to enter an immersive view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-355">選取 [允許]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-355">Select **Allow**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-356">[點擊](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) 以顯示播放控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-356">[Air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to bring up the playback controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-357">使用 [光線和空中](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) 點來播放/暫停、向前/向後跳過、開啟/關閉字幕，或停止 (的體驗，以) 離開沉浸式視圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-357">Use [hand rays and air tap](hololens2-basic-usage.md#select-using-air-tap) to play/pause, skip forward/back, turn captions on/off, or stop the experience (which exits the immersive view).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-358">播放控制項將會在幾秒鐘的非使用狀態後消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-358">The playback controls will disappear after a few seconds of inactivity.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-webxr-and-360-viewer-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-359">頂尖 WebXR 和360檢視器的已知問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-359">Top WebXR and 360 Viewer known issues</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-360">根據 WebXR 體驗的複雜度而定，畫面播放速率可能會下降或斷斷續續。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-360">Depending on the complexity of the WebXR experience, the framerate may drop or stutter.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-361">依預設，不會啟用 WebXR 中所述的手接頭支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-361">Support for articulated hand joints in WebXR is not enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-362">開發人員可以藉 `edge://flags` 由開啟「WebXR 手輸入」來啟用支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-362">Developers can enable support via `edge://flags` by turning on "WebXR Hand Input."</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-363">來自 YouTube 以外網站的360影片可能無法如預期般運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-363">360 videos from websites other than YouTube may not work as expected.</span></span>

#### <a name="providing-feedback-on-webxr-and-360-viewer"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-364">在 WebXR 和360檢視器上提供意見反應</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-364">Providing feedback on WebXR and 360 Viewer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-365">請透過新的 Microsoft Edge 中的 [**傳送意見** 反應] 功能，與我們的小組分享意見反應和 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-365">Please share feedback and bugs with our team via the **Send Feedback** feature in the new Microsoft Edge.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-366">新增設定應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-366">New Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-367">在此版本中，我們引進了新版的設定應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-367">With this release, we're introducing a new version of the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-368">新的設定應用程式包括下欄區域中 HoloLens 2 的新功能和展開的設定：音效、電源 & 睡眠、網路 & 網際網路、應用程式、帳戶、輕鬆存取等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-368">The new Settings app includes new features and expanded settings for HoloLens 2 in the following areas: Sound, Power & sleep, Network & Internet, Apps, Accounts, Ease of Access, and more.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-369">因為新的設定應用程式與舊版設定應用程式不同，所以您先前在環境中放置的任何設定視窗將會在更新時移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-369">Because the new Settings app is distinct from the legacy Settings app, any Settings windows you previously placed around your environment will be removed upon update.</span></span>

![新的設定應用程式首頁](images/new-settings-app.png)

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-371">**新功能與設定**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-371">**New features and settings**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-372">設定搜尋：使用關鍵字或設定的名稱，從設定首頁搜尋設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-372">Settings search: search for settings from the Settings homepage using keywords or the setting's name.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-373">系統 > 音效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-373">System > Sound:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-374">輸入和輸出音訊裝置：個別選擇您的輸入和輸出音訊裝置 (例如，透過藍牙耳機聆聽音訊，或針對音訊輸入) 使用 USB-C 麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-374">Input and output audio devices: independently choose your input and output audio devices (for example, listen to audio via Bluetooth headphones or use a USB-C microphone for audio input).</span></span>
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="8175b-375">HoloLens 2 不支援藍牙的麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-375">Bluetooth microphones are not supported by HoloLens 2.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-376">應用程式磁片區：個別調整每個應用程式的磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-376">App volume: independently adjust the volume of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-377">請參閱 [每個應用程式音量控制](#per-app-volume-control)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-377">See [per app volume control](#per-app-volume-control).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-378">系統 > 電源 & 睡眠：選擇裝置在閒置一段時間後應進入睡眠狀態的時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-378">System > Power & sleep: choose when the device should go to sleep after a period of inactivity.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-379">系統 > 電池：以手動方式啟用省電模式模式，或設定省電模式模式自動開啟的電池閾值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-379">System > Battery: manually enable battery saver mode or set a battery threshold at which point battery saver mode turns on automatically.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-380">裝置 > USB：您預設可以停用 USB 連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-380">Devices > USB: you can disable USB connections by default.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-381">網路 & 網際網路：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-381">Network & Internet:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-382">USB 乙太網路介面卡現在會出現在 Network & Internet 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-382">USB-C Ethernet adapters will now appear in Network & Internet.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-383">現在已可使用 USB 乙太網路介面卡設定，包括其 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-383">USB-C Ethernet adapter settings are now available, including its IP address.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-384">您現在可以在 HoloLens 2 上啟用飛機模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-384">You can now enable airplane mode on HoloLens 2.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-385">應用程式：您可以重設用於檔案和連結類型的預設應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-385">Apps: you can reset the default apps used for file and link types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-386">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [預設應用程式選擇器](#default-app-picker)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-386">For more information see [Default app picker](#default-app-picker).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-387">帳戶 > 其他使用者：裝置擁有者可以新增使用者、將標準使用者升級為裝置擁有者、將裝置擁有者降級為標準使用者，以及移除使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-387">Accounts > Other users: device owners can add users, upgrade standard users to device owners, downgrade device owners to standard users, and remove users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-388">輕鬆存取：變更文字大小和某些視覺效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-388">Ease of Access: change text size and some visual effects.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-389">**已知問題**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-389">**Known issues**</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-390">先前放置設定 windows 將會移除 (請參閱上述) 的附注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-390">Previously placed Settings windows will be removed (see note above).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-391">您無法再使用設定應用程式重新命名您的裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-391">You can no longer rename your device with the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-392">IT 系統管理員可以使用 HoloLens 2 裝置名稱範本的[Windows Autopilot](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot)或 MDM [DevDetail CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName 節點來重新命名裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-392">IT admins can rename devices by using the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot) device name template or the MDM [DevDetail CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/devdetail-csp) Ext/Microsoft/DNSComputerName node.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-393">[乙太網路] 頁面會 ( [UsbNcm] ) 隨時顯示虛擬乙太網路裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-393">The Ethernet page shows a virtual Ethernet device ("UsbNcm") at all times.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-394">新 Microsoft Edge 的電池使用量可能不准確，因為它的本質是 UWP 介面卡層所支援的 Win32 桌面應用程式 (不會在) 中預期任何修正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-394">Battery usage for the new Microsoft Edge may not be accurate, due to its nature as a Win32 desktop application supported by a UWP adapter layer (no fix anticipated soon).</span></span>

#### <a name="display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-395">顯示色彩校正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-395">Display color calibration</span></span>



<span data-ttu-id="8175b-396">使用這個新的設定，您可以選取 HoloLens 2 顯示的替代色彩設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-396">With this new setting, you can select an alternative color profile for your HoloLens 2 display.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-397">這可能有助於更精確地顯示色彩，特別是在較低的顯示器亮度等級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-397">This may help colors appear more accurate, especially at lower display brightness levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-398">您可以在 [系統 > 校正] 頁面上的設定應用程式中找到顯示器色彩校正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-398">Display color calibration can be found in the Settings app, on the System > Calibration page.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-399">因為此設定會將新的色彩設定檔儲存到您的顯示器固件，所以會有每個裝置的設定 (而且不是每個使用者帳戶) 的唯一設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-399">Because this setting saves a new color profile to your display firmware, it is a per-device setting (and not unique to each user account).</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-use-display-color-calibration"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-400">如何使用顯示器色彩校正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-400">How to use display color calibration</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-401">啟動 **設定** 應用程式，並流覽至 [**系統 > 校正**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-401">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-402">在 [ **顯示色彩校正**] 下，選取 [ **執行顯示器色彩校正** ] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-402">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Run display color calibration** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-403">顯示色彩校正體驗將會啟動，並建議您確認您的面板是否位於正確的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-403">The display color calibration experience will launch and encourage you to make sure your visor is in the correct position.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-404">在您繼續進行 [指示] 對話方塊之後，您的顯示器會自動呈現為30% 的亮度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-404">After you proceed through the instruction dialog boxes, your display will automatically be dimmed to 30% brightness.</span></span>
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="8175b-405">如果您在環境中看到灰色的場景時發生問題，您可以使用裝置左邊的亮度按鈕，手動調整 HoloLens 2 的亮度等級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-405">If you're having trouble seeing the dimmed scene in your environment, you can manually adjust the brightness level of HoloLens 2 using the brightness buttons on the left side of the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-406">選取按鈕1-6 以立即試用每個色彩設定檔，並找出看起來最適合您的眼睛 (這通常表示可協助場景顯示最中性的設定檔，且灰階模式和外觀色調會如預期般顯示。 ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-406">Select buttons 1-6 to instantly try out each color profile, and find one that looks the best to your eyes (this usually means the profile that helps the scene appear most neutral, with the grayscale pattern and skin tones looking as expected.)</span></span>

    ![顯示色彩校正場景](images/color-cal-ui.png)
    
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-408">當您對選取的設定檔感到滿意時，請選取 [ **儲存 &** 結束] 按鈕</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-408">When you're happy with the selected profile, select the **Save & Exit** button</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-409">如果您不想要進行變更，請選取 [ **取消 &** 結束] 按鈕，您的變更將會還原</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-409">If you prefer not to make changes, select the **Cancel & Exit** button and your changes will be reverted</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-410">以下是使用顯示色彩校正設定時要牢記在心的一些實用秘訣：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-410">Here are some helpful tips to keep in mind while using the display color calibration setting:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-411">您可以視需要從設定重新執行顯示器色彩校正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-411">You can re-run display color calibration from Settings whenever you'd like</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-412">如果裝置上的任何人先前使用設定來變更色彩設定檔，則最近變更的日期/時間會反映在設定頁面上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-412">If anyone on the device has previously used the setting to change color profiles, the date/time of the most recent change will be reflected on the Settings page</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-413">當您重新執行顯示器色彩校正時，會反白顯示先前儲存的色彩設定檔，而且不會出現設定檔 0 (因為設定檔0代表顯示器的原始色彩設定檔) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-413">When you re-run display color calibration, the color profile that was previously saved will be highlighted and Profile 0 will not appear (as Profile 0 represents the display's original color profile)</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-414">如果您想要還原成顯示器的原始色彩設定檔，您可以從設定頁面 (查看[如何重設色彩設定檔](#how-to-reset-color-profile)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-414">If you want to revert to the display's original color profile, you can do so from the Settings page (see [how to reset color profile](#how-to-reset-color-profile))</span></span>

##### <a name="how-to-reset-color-profile"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-415">如何重設色彩設定檔</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-415">How to reset color profile</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-416">如果您不滿意將自訂色彩設定檔儲存到您的 HoloLens 2，您可以還原裝置的原始色彩設定檔：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-416">If you're unhappy with the custom color profile saved to your HoloLens 2, you can restore the device's original color profile:</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-417">啟動 **設定** 應用程式，並流覽至 [**系統 > 校正**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-417">Launch the **Settings** app and navigate to **System > Calibration**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-418">在 [ **顯示色彩校正**] 下，選取 [ **重設為預設色彩設定檔** ] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-418">Under **Display color calibration**, select the **Reset to default color profile** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-419">當對話方塊開啟時，如果您已準備好重新開機 HoloLens 2 並套用變更，請選取 [**重新開機**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-419">When the dialog box opens, select **Restart** if you're ready to restart HoloLens 2 and apply your changes.</span></span>

#### <a name="top-display-color-calibration-known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-420">最常見的顯示器色彩校正已知問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-420">Top display color calibration known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-421">在 [設定] 頁面上，在您將該頁面重載設定之前，會告知您上次變更色彩設定檔的狀態字串將會過期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-421">On the Settings page, the status string that tells you when the color profile was last changed will be out of date until you reload that page of Settings.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-422">因應措施：選取另一個設定頁面，然後重新選取 [校正] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-422">Workaround: Select another Settings page and then re-select the Calibration page.</span></span>

#### <a name="default-app-picker"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-423">預設應用程式選擇器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-423">Default app picker</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-424">當您啟用超連結或開啟具有多個已安裝應用程式的檔案類型（支援它）時，您會看到新的視窗開啟，提示您選取哪些已安裝的應用程式應該處理檔案或連結類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-424">When you activate a hyperlink or open a file type with more than one installed app, which supports it, you will see a new window open prompting you to select which installed app should handle the file or link type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-425">在此視窗中，您也可以選擇讓選取的應用程式處理檔案或連結類型「一次」或「一律」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-425">In this window, you can also choose to have the selected app handle the file or link type "Once" or "Always."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-426">如果您選擇 [永遠]，但稍後想要變更哪個應用程式會處理特定的檔案或連結類型，您可以在 **設定 > 應用程式** 中重設已儲存的預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-426">If you choose "Always" but later want to change which app handles a particular file or link type, you can reset your saved defaults in **Settings > Apps**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-427">滾動至頁面底部，然後選取 [檔案類型的預設應用程式] 和/或 [連結類型的預設應用程式] 下的 [ **清除** ] 按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-427">Scroll to the bottom of the page and select the **Clear** button under "Default apps for file types" and/or "Default apps for link types."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-428">不同于桌上型電腦上的類似設定，您無法重設個別的檔案類型預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-428">Unlike the similar setting on desktop PCs, you can't reset individual file type defaults.</span></span>

#### <a name="per-app-volume-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-429">每個應用程式音量控制項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-429">Per app volume control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-430">現在在此 Windows 組建中，使用者可以手動調整每個應用程式的音量層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-430">Now in this Windows build, users can manually adjust the volume level of each app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-431">這可讓使用者更專注于所需的應用程式，或在使用多個應用程式時更容易聽到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-431">This allows for users to better focus on the apps that they need to, or better hear when using multiple apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-432">例如，需要在另一個應用程式中呼叫另一個應用程式來提供遠端協助時，關閉其中一個應用程式的容量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-432">Such as needing to turn down volume of one app while calling another person for remote assistance in another.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-433">若要設定個別應用程式的音量，請流覽至 **設定**  ->  **系統**  ->  **音效**，並在 [Advanced 音效選項] 下選取 [**應用程式磁片區和裝置喜好** 設定]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-433">To set the volume of an individual app navigate to **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, and under Advanced sound options select **App volume and device preferences**.</span></span><br/><br/>

<img alt="App volume and device preferences." src="./images/volume-per-app.jpg" width="500" height="250" />

#### <a name="swipe-to-type"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-434">滑動至類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-434">Swipe to type</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-435">有些客戶會透過輕量其想要輸入的單字圖形，來更快速地「輸入」虛擬鍵盤，而且我們要預覽全像全像鍵盤的這項功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-435">Some customers find it faster to "type" on virtual keyboards by swiping the shape of the word they intend to type, and we're previewing this feature for the holographic keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-436">您可以一次滑動一個單字，方法是將手指的筆尖傳遞到全像全像鍵盤的平面，然後將該單字的形狀輕量，然後從鍵盤的平面提款手指的秘訣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-436">You can swipe one word at a time by passing the tip of your finger through the plane of the holographic keyboard, swiping the shape of the word, and then withdrawing the tip of your finger from the plane of the keyboard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-437">您可以在文字之間，從鍵盤中移除手指，而不需要按下空格鍵，就可以將文字滑行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-437">You can swipe follow up words without needing to press the space bar by removing your finger from the keyboard between words.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-438">如果您在鍵盤上的手指移動之後看到滑動軌跡，您將會知道此功能是否正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-438">You will know the feature is working if you see a swipe trail following your finger's movement on the keyboard.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-439">請注意，這項功能可能很難使用，主要是因為全像攝影鍵盤的本質，您不覺得像行動電話顯示器) ，因此不會對手指 (感到阻力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-439">Please note, this feature can be tricky to use and master because of the nature of a holographic keyboard where you don't feel resistance against your finger (unlike a mobile phone display).</span></span> 

### <a name="power-menu-from-start"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-440">從開始的電源功能表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-440">Power menu from Start</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-441">新的功能表，可讓使用者登出、關閉及重新開機裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-441">A new menu that allows the user to sign out, shut down and restart the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-442">HoloLens 開始畫面中的指標，會顯示可用的系統更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-442">An indicator in the HoloLens Start screen that shows when a system update is available.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-use"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-443">如何使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-443">How to use</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-444">使用[開始手勢](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture)開啟 HoloLens 開始畫面，或說「移至開始」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-444">Open the HoloLens Start screen using the [Start gesture](hololens2-basic-usage.md#start-gesture) or saying "Go to Start".</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-445">請注意，[使用者設定檔] 圖片旁的省略號圖示 ( ... ) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-445">Notice the ellipsis icon (...) next to the user profile picture:</span></span><br/><br/>

   <img alt="ser context dots, ..." src="./images/powertransition_icon_default_cropped.png" width="586" height="330" />

3. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-446">使用您的手或語音命令「電源」來選取使用者個人資料圖片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-446">Select the user profile picture using your hands or the voice command "Power".</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-447">隨即出現一個功能表，其中包含登出、重新開機或關閉裝置的選項：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-447">A menu appears with options to Sign out, Restart or Shut down the device:</span></span><br/><br/>

   <img alt="User context menu" src="./images/powertransition_aad_options_cropped.png" width="586" height="330" />

5. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-448">選取要登出、重新開機或關閉 HoloLens 的功能表選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-448">Select the menu options to sign out, restart or shut down your HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-449">如果裝置設定為 [單一 Microsoft 帳戶 (MSA) 或本機帳戶](hololens-identity.md)，則可能無法使用 [登出] 選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-449">The Sign out option might not be available, if the device is set up for a [single Microsoft Account (MSA) or local account](hololens-identity.md).</span></span>

6. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-450">使用開始手勢觸及任何其他地方或關閉 [開始] 功能表，以關閉功能表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-450">Dismiss the menu by touching anywhere else or closing the Start menu with the Start gesture.</span></span>

#### <a name="update-indicator"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-451">更新指標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-451">Update indicator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-452">當有可用的更新時，省略號圖示會很亮，表示重新開機將會安裝更新。功能表選項也會變更，以反映更新是否存在。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-452">When an update is available, the ellipsis icon will light up to indicate that a restart will install the update The menu options also change to reflect the presence of the update.</span></span><br/><br/>

### <a name="multiple-users-listed-on-sign-in-screen"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-453">登入畫面上列出多個使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-453">Multiple users listed on Sign in screen</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-454">先前的 [登入] 畫面只會顯示最近登入的使用者，以及「其他使用者」進入點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-454">Previously the Sign In screen showed only the most recently signed in user, as well as an 'Other user' entry point.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-455">如果有多位使用者登入裝置，就會收到客戶的意見反應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-455">We have received customer feedback that this not sufficient if multiple users have signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-456">他們仍然需要重新輸入使用者名稱等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-456">They were still required to retype their username etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-457">在此 Windows 組建中引進，當選取 [PIN 輸入] 欄位右邊的 **其他使用者** 時，[登入] 畫面會顯示多個先前已登入裝置的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-457">Introduced in this Windows build, when selecting **Other user** which is located to the right of the PIN entry field, the Sign in screen will display multiple users with have previously signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-458">這可讓使用者選取其使用者設定檔，然後使用其 Windows Hello 認證進行登入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-458">This allows users to select their user profile and then sign-in using their Windows Hello credentials.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-459">您也可以透過 [新增 **帳戶** ] 按鈕，從 [其他使用者] 頁面將新的使用者新增至裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-459">A new user can also be added to the device from this Other users page via the **Add account** button.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-460">在 [其他使用者] 功能表中，[其他使用者] 按鈕會顯示上次登入裝置的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-460">When in the Other users menu, the Other users button will display the last user signed into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-461">選取此按鈕，返回此使用者的登入畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-461">Select this button to return to the Sign in screen for this user.</span></span>

### <a name="usb-c-external-microphone-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-464">USB-C 外部麥克風支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-464">USB-C External Microphone Support</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-465">插入 **USB mic 並不會自動將它設定為輸入裝置**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-465">Plugging in **a USB mic will not automatically set it as the input device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-466">當插入一組 USB-C 耳機時，系統會注意到耳機的音訊將會自動重新導向到耳機，但 HoloLens OS 會將內部麥克風陣列的優先順序排列在任何其他輸入裝置上方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-466">When plugging in a set of USB-C headphones users will observe that the headphone's audio will automatically be redirected to the headphones, but the HoloLens OS prioritizes the internal microphone array above any other input device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-467">**若要使用 USB 麥克風，請遵循下列步驟。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-467">**In order to use a USB-C microphone follow the steps below.**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-468">使用者可以使用 [ **音效** 設定] 面板來選取 USB-C 連接的外部麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-468">Users can select USB-C connected external microphones using the **Sound** settings panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-469">USB-C 麥克風可以用來呼叫、錄製等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-469">USB-C microphones can be used for calling, recording, etc.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-470">開啟 **設定** 應用程式，然後選取 [**系統**  >  **音效**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-470">Open the **Settings** app and select **System** > **Sound**.</span></span>

![音效設定](images/usbc-mic-1.jpg)

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-472">若要搭配使用外部麥克風與 **遠端協助**，使用者必須按一下 [管理音效裝置] 超連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-472">To use external microphones with **Remote Assist**, users will need to click the “Manage sound devices” hyperlink.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-473">然後使用下拉式清單將外部麥克風設定為 [ **預設** ] 或 [ **通訊] 預設值。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-473">Then use the drop-down to set the external microphone as either **Default** or **Communications Default.**</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-474">選擇 [ **預設值** ] 表示外部麥克風將用於所有位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-474">Choosing **Default** means that the external microphone will be used everywhere.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-475">選擇 [**通訊預設值**] 表示外部麥克風將用於遠端協助和其他通訊應用程式，但 HoloLens mic 陣列仍可用於其他工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-475">Choosing **Communications Default** means that the external microphone will be used in Remote Assist and other communications apps, but the HoloLens mic array may still be used for other tasks.</span></span>

![管理音效裝置](images/usbc-mic-2.png)
