#### <a name="what-about-bluetooth-microphone-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-478">藍牙麥克風支援呢？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-478">What about Bluetooth microphone support?</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-479">不幸的是，HoloLens 2 上目前仍不支援藍牙的麥克風。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-479">Unfortunately Bluetooth microphones are still not currently supported on HoloLens 2.</span></span>

#### <a name="troubleshooting-usb-c-microphones"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-480">疑難排解 USB-C 麥克風</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-480">Troubleshooting USB-C microphones</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-481">請注意，某些 USB C 麥克風錯誤地將本身視為麥克風 *和* 說話者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-481">Be aware that some USB-C microphones incorrectly report themselves as both a microphone *and* a speaker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-482">這是麥克風的問題，而不是 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-482">This is a problem with the microphone and not with HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-483">將其中一個麥克風插入 HoloLens 時，可能會遺失音效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-483">When plugging one of these microphones into HoloLens, sound may be lost.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-484">幸運的是，有一個簡單的修正程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-484">Fortunately there is a simple fix.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-485">在 **設定**  ->  **系統**  ->  **音效** 中，將內建的喇叭 **(模擬功能音訊驅動程式)** 明確設定為 **預設裝置**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-485">In **Settings** -> **System** -> **Sound**, explicitly set the built-in speakers **(Analog Feature Audio Driver)** as the **Default device**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-486">HoloLens 應該記得這項設定，即使稍後移除並重新連線麥克風也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-486">HoloLens should remember this setting even if the microphone is removed and reconnected later.</span></span>

![疑難排解 USB-C 麥克風](images/usbc-mic-4.png)

### <a name="visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-488">Kiosk 的訪客自動登入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-488">Visitor Auto logon for Kiosks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-489">這項新功能可讓造訪者帳戶使用自動登入，以用於 Kiosk 模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-489">This new feature enables the auto logon on Visitor accounts to be used for Kiosk modes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-490">針對非 AAD 設定，設定裝置以進行訪客自動登入：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-490">For a non-AAD configuration, to configure a device for visitor auto-logon:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-491">建立提供者的布建套件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-491">Create a provisioning package that:</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-492">**設定執行時間設定/>assignedaccess** ，以允許訪客帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-492">Configures **Runtime settings/AssignedAccess** to allow Visitor accounts.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-493">您可以選擇性地在 MDM 中註冊裝置 **(執行時間設定/工作場所/註冊)** ，以便稍後進行管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-493">Optionally enrolls the device in MDM **(Runtime settings/Workplace/Enrollments)** so that it can be managed later.</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-494">請勿建立本機帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-494">Do not create a local account</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-495">套用布建[套件](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-495">[Apply the provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-496">針對 AAD 設定，使用者現在可以在沒有這項變更的情況下，達成與此類似的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-496">For an AAD configuration, users can achieve something similar to this today without this change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-497">針對 kiosk 模式設定的已加入 AAD 裝置，可以透過單一按鈕，從登入畫面登入造訪者帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-497">AAD joined devices configured for kiosk mode can sign in a Visitor account with a single button tap from the sign in screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-498">登入訪客帳戶之後，裝置將不會再次提示您登入，直到造訪者明確登出 [開始] 功能表或重新開機裝置為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-498">Once signed in to the visitor account, the device will not prompt for sign in again until the Visitor is explicitly signed out from the start menu or the device is restarted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-499">您可以透過 [自訂 oma-uri](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) 原則來管理訪客自動登入：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-499">Visitor Auto logon can be managed via [custom OMA-URI](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/intune/configuration/custom-settings-windows-10) policy:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-500">URI 值：./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-500">URI value: ./Device/Vendor/MSFT/MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-501">原則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-501">Policy</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-502">描述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-502">Description</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-503">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-503">Configurations</span></span>  |
|---|---|---|
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-504">MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-504">MixedReality/VisitorAutoLogon</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-505">允許訪客自動登入 Kiosk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-505">Allows for a Visitor to Auto logon to a Kiosk</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-506">1 (是) ，0 (否，預設值。 ) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-506">1 (Yes), 0 (No, default.)</span></span>  |

### <a name="use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-507">在 Kiosk 模式中使用新的設定和 Edge 應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-507">Use the new Settings and Edge apps in Kiosk modes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-508">在 kiosk 中包含應用程式 [時，IT](hololens-kiosk.md)系統管理員通常會將應用程式新增至 Kiosk，但使用它的應用程式使用者模型識別碼 (AUMID) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-508">When including apps in [Kiosks](hololens-kiosk.md), an IT Admin often adds the app to the Kiosk but using it's App User Model ID (AUMID).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-509">因為設定應用程式和 Microsoft Edge 應用程式都被視為新的應用程式，而且不同于使用 aumid 來執行這些應用程式的繼承應用程式 kiosk，所以必須更新為使用新的 AUMID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-509">Because both the Settings app and Microsoft Edge app are considered new apps and different than the older apps Kiosks that use AUMIDs for those apps will need to be updated to use the new AUMID.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-510">修改 Kiosk 以包含新的應用程式時，建議您加入新的 AUMID，並保留舊的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-510">When modifying a Kiosk to include the new apps, we recommend adding in the new AUMID as well as leaving the old one.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-511">當使用者更新作業系統時，這將會建立簡單的轉換，而不需要接收新的原則以繼續使用 Kiosk。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-511">This will create an easy transition when users update the OS and won't need to receive new policies to keep using the Kiosk as intended.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-512">應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-512">App</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-513">AUMID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-513">AUMID</span></span>                                                  |
|------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-514">舊的設定應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-514">Old Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-515">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy！應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-515">HolographicSystemSettings_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span>            |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-516">新增設定應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-516">New Settings App</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-517">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-800B-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy！應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-517">BAEAEF15-9BAB-47FC-800B-ACECAD2AE94B_cw5n1h2txyewy!App</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-518">舊的 Microsoft Edge 應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-518">Old Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-519">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-519">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-520">新增 Microsoft Edge 應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-520">New Microsoft Edge app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-521">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe！X-MSEDGE-CLIENTID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-521">Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge.Stable_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MSEDGE</span></span>    |

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-522">處理失敗的 Kiosk 模式行為變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-522">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-523">在較舊的組建中，如果裝置的 kiosk 設定是全域指派的存取權和 AAD 群組成員指派的存取權，則如果判斷 AAD 群組成員資格失敗，使用者會看到 [[開始] 功能表中顯示 [沒有任何內容](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-523">In older builds, if a device had a kiosk configuration, which is a combination of both global assigned access and AAD group member assigned access, if determining AAD group membership failed, the user would see “[nothing shown in start](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-kiosk#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)” menu.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-524">從這個 Windows 版本開始，如果在 AAD 群組 kiosk 模式期間發生失敗，則 kiosk 體驗將會回復為全域 kiosk 設定 (（如果有) 的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-524">Starting in this Windows release, the kiosk experience will fallback to global kiosk configuration (if present) in case of failures during AAD group kiosk mode.</span></span>

### <a name="new-settings-uris-for-page-settings-visibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-525">頁面設定可見度的新設定 uri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-525">New Settings URIs for Page Settings Visibility</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-526">在[Windows 全像20H2 版中，](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2)我們新增了[設定/PageVisibilityList 原則](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist)，以限制在設定應用程式中看到的頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-526">In [Windows Holographic, version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2) we added the [Settings/PageVisibilityList policy](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-settings#settings-pagevisibilitylist) to restrict the pages seen within the Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-527">PageVisibilityList 是一項原則，可讓 IT 系統管理員防止系統設定應用程式中的特定頁面被顯示或存取，或針對所有頁面（除了指定的頁面以外）進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-527">PageVisibilityList is a policy that allows IT Admins to either prevent specific pages in the System Settings app from being visible or accessible, or to do so for all pages except those specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-528">如果您造訪[頁面設定可見度](settings-uri-list.md)，您可以找到使用此 CSP 的指示，以及先前版本中可用的 uri 清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-528">If you visit [Page Settings Visibility](settings-uri-list.md), you can find instructions to use this CSP and the list of URIs available in previous releases.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-529">我們會根據可供 IT 系統管理員管理的可用設定 uri 清單來擴充。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-529">We are expanding upon the list of list of available Settings URIs, which IT Admins can manage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-530">其中一些 Uri 適用于新的設定應用程式內新的可用區域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-530">Some of these URIs are for newly available areas within the new Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-531">如果您使用設定/PageVisibilityList 原則，請檢查下列清單，並視需要調整您允許或封鎖的頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-531">If you are using Settings/PageVisibilityList policy, review the following list and adjust your allowed or blocked pages as needed.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-532">**已淘汰： ms 設定：網路-proxy**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-532">**Deprecated: ms-settings:network-proxy**</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-533">在這些較新的組建中，其中一個設定頁面已被取代。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-533">One settings page is deprecated in these newer builds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-534">舊的 **網路 & [網際網路**  >  **Proxy** ] 頁面已不再以全域設定的形式提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-534">The old **Network & Internet** > **Proxy** page is no longer available as a global setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-535">新的每個連線 proxy 設定可以在 **network & internet**  >  **wi-fi**  >  **properties** 或 **network & 網際網路**  >  **乙太** 網路內容中找到  >  \*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-535">The new per-connection proxy settings can be found under **Network & Internet** > **Wi-Fi** > **Properties** or **Network & Internet** > **Ethernet** > **Properties**.</span></span>

#### <a name="updated-uris"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-561">更新的 Uri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-561">Updated URIs</span></span>

- `ms-settings:windowsupdate-options`
- `ms-settings:windowsupdate-restartoptions`

### <a name="configuring-fallback-diagnostics-via-settings-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-564">透過設定應用程式設定 Fallback 診斷</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-564">Configuring Fallback Diagnostics via Settings app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-565">現在在設定應用程式中，使用者可以設定[Fallback 診斷](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md)的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-565">Now in Settings App, a user can configure the behavior of [Fallback Diagnostics](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-566">在設定應用程式中，流覽至 **隱私權**  ->  **疑難排解** 頁面以設定此設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-566">In the Settings app navigate to **Privacy** -> **Troubleshooting** page to configure this setting.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-567">如果裝置已設定 MDM 原則，使用者將無法覆寫該行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-567">If there is MDM policy configured for the device, user will not be able to override that behavior.</span></span>  

### <a name="share-things-with-nearby-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-568">與附近裝置共用事物</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-568">Share things with nearby devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-569">Windows 10 裝置（包括電腦和其他 HoloLens 2 裝置）分享相關專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-569">Share things with near by Windows 10 devices, including both PCs and other HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-570">您可以在 **設定**  ->  **系統**  ->  **共用體驗** 中試用，以從 HoloLens 共用檔案或 url 至電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-570">You can try it out in **Settings** -> **System** -> **Shared Experiences** to share files or URLs from a HoloLens to a PC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-571">如需詳細資訊，請閱讀更多有關如何[在 Windows 10 中與附近裝置共用內容](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9)的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-571">For more details read more about how to [Share things with nearby devices in Windows 10](https://support.microsoft.com/windows/share-things-with-nearby-devices-in-windows-10-0efbfe40-e3e2-581b-13f4-1a0e9936c2d9).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-572">這項功能可以透過 [Connectivity/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices)管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-572">This feature can be managed via [Connectivity/AllowConnectedDevices](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowconnecteddevices).</span></span>

### <a name="new-os-diagnostic-traces"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-573">新的作業系統診斷追蹤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-573">New OS diagnostic traces</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-574">除了設定應用程式內先前的疑難排解工具之外，還新增了新的疑難排解員，新增了新的設定應用程式以進行 OS 更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-574">In addition to the previous troubleshooters within the Settings app, a new troubleshooter has been added with the addition of the new Settings app for OS Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-575">流覽至 **設定**  ->  **更新 &amp; 安全性**  >  **疑難排解**  >  **Windows Update** ，然後選取 [**啟動**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-575">Navigate to **Settings** -> **Update &amp; Security** > **Troubleshoot** > **Windows Update** and select **Start**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-576">這可讓您在使用作業系統更新重現問題時收集追蹤，以協助您更妥善地針對 IT 或支援進行疑難排解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-576">This allows you to collect traces while reproducing your issue with OS Updates to assist better in troubleshooting with your IT or support.</span></span>

### <a name="delivery-optimization-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-577">傳遞最佳化預覽</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-577">Delivery Optimization Preview</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-578">透過此 HoloLens 更新，Windows Holographic for Business 可啟用傳遞優化設定，以減少從多個 HoloLens 裝置下載的頻寬耗用量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-578">With this HoloLens update, Windows Holographic for Business enables delivery optimization settings to reduce bandwidth consumption for downloads from multiple HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-579">您可以在這裡找到這項功能的完整說明，以及建議的網路設定： [Windows 10 更新的傳遞最佳化](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-579">A fuller description of this functionality along with the recommended network configuration is available here: [Delivery Optimization for Windows 10 updates](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-594">Windows Holographic for Business 僅支援來自[Microsoft 網內快取端點](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/configmgr/core/plan-design/hierarchy/microsoft-connected-cache)的 HTTP 下載模式和下載;目前不支援對等下載模式和群組指派的 HoloLens 裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-594">Windows Holographic for Business only supports HTTP download modes and downloads from a [Microsoft Connected Cache endpoint](https://docs.microsoft.com/mem/configmgr/core/plan-design/hierarchy/microsoft-connected-cache); peer-to-peer download modes and group assignments are not supported for HoloLens devices at this time.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-595">HoloLens 不支援 Windows Server Update Services 端點的部署或傳遞優化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-595">HoloLens does not support deployment or delivery optimization for Windows Server Update Services endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-596">疑難排解將需要網內快取伺服器上的診斷，或透過 **設定**  >  **Update & 安全性**  >   **疑難排解**  >   **Windows Update**，在 HoloLens 上 HoloLens 收集追蹤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-596">Troubleshooting will require either diagnostics on the Connected Cache server or collecting a trace on HoloLens on HoloLens via **Settings** > **Update & Security** >  **Troubleshooting** >  **Windows Update**.</span></span>

### <a name="it-admin---update-checklist"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-597">IT 系統管理員-更新檢查清單</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-597">IT Admin - Update Checklist</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-598">這份檢查清單可協助您瞭解此功能更新中新增的功能，這項功能可能會影響您目前的裝置管理設定，或您可能想要開始使用的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-598">This checklist will help you know the new items that features that are being added in this feature update that may affect your current device management configurations, or new features you might wish to start using.</span></span>

#### <a name="updates-to-kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-599">Kiosk 模式的更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-599">Updates to Kiosk mode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-600">[**在 Kiosk 模式中為新的應用程式✔️新 aumid**](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-600">✔️ [**New AUMIDs for new apps in Kiosk mode**](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-601">如果您先前在 Kiosk 中使用設定應用程式或 Microsoft Edge 應用程式，我們已將這些應用程式取代為使用不同應用程式識別碼的新應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-601">If you were previously using either the Settings app or Microsoft Edge app in a Kiosk, we have replaced these apps with new apps which use a different App ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-602">強烈建議您 [在下方的 Kiosk 模式中，為新的應用程式閱讀新的 aumid](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-602">We highly encourage you to read [New AUMIDs for new apps in Kiosk mode](#use-the-new-settings-and-edge-apps-in-kiosk-modes) below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-603">這可確保您在 Kiosk 中繼續設定的應用程式，或加入新的 Microsoft Edge 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-603">This will ensure you either continue to have the Settings app in your Kiosk, or include the new Microsoft Edge app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-604">您現在可以完成這些變更，並將其部署到所有裝置，並允許在更新時進行更順暢的轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-604">These changes can be done now, and deployed to all devices and allow for a smoother transition on update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-605">✔️ [**kiosk 的訪客自動登入**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks)：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-605">✔️ [**Visitor Auto-logon for Kiosks**](#visitor-auto-logon-for-kiosks):</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-606">訪客現在可以自動登入 Kiosk。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-606">Visitors can now be automatically logged into a Kiosk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-607">此行為預設為開啟，但可以進行管理和停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-607">This behavior is on by default but can be managed and disabled.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-608">✔️ [**改良的 Kiosk 模式失敗**](#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures)處理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-608">✔️ [**Improved Kiosk mode failure handing**](#kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-609">如果未成功判斷登入 AAD 使用者的 AAD 群組成員資格，則會在 [開始] 功能表 (使用全域 kiosk 設定（如果) 有的話），否則使用者會看到空白的 [開始] 功能表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-609">If AAD group membership of signed-in AAD user is not successfully determined, then global kiosk configuration is used for start menu (if present) otherwise user is presented with empty start menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-610">雖然空白的 [開始] 功能表不是您可以直接設定的設定，但這項新的處理可能是在使用 Kiosk 時通知您支援部門的事項，因為這可能適用于您的設定，或者您可能會想要對指派的存取設定進行新調整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-610">While the empty start menu is not a configuration you can directly set, this new handling may be something to inform your support department of if you are using Kiosks, as this may apply to your configurations or you may want to make new adjustments to your assigned access configurations.</span></span>

#### <a name="updates-to-page-settings-visibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-611">設定可見度的頁面更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-611">Updates to Page Settings Visibility</span></span>

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-625">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-625">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-626">[離線診斷](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md#offline-diagnostics) 也會包含序號和 OS 版本的其他裝置資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-626">[Offline diagnostics](hololens-diagnostic-logs.md#offline-diagnostics) will also include additional device information for serial number and OS version.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-627">修正透過執行時間布建套件部署企業營運應用程式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-627">Fixes an issue around deployment of line of business applications via runtime provisioning packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-628">修正有關企業營運應用程式安裝狀態報表的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-628">Fixes an issue around line of business application install status reporting.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-629">修正跨裝置重設期間新應用程式套件持續性的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-629">Fixes an issue around the persistence of new app packages across device resets.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-630">修正可能導致在 Edge 中為日文客戶輸入錯誤符號的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-630">Fixes an issue that could lead to incorrect symbols being typed in Edge for Japanese customers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-631">改善在預先安裝的應用程式（例如 Edge）周圍作業系統更新的復原能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-631">Improves the resiliency of OS updates around preinstalled apps such as Edge.</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-632">解決影響 Microsoft Edge 安裝的更新可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-632">Addresses an update reliability impacting the installation of Microsoft Edge.</span></span> 


## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2--may-2021-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-633">Windows全像20H2 版-5 月2021更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-633">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – May 2021 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-634">組建19041.1146</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-634">Build 19041.1146</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-635">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-635">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

### <a name="install-apps-on-hololens-2-via-app-installer"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-680">透過應用程式安裝程式在 HoloLens 2 上安裝應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-680">Install Apps on HoloLens 2 via App Installer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-681">我們 **新增了 (應用程式安裝程式) 的新功能，可讓您更順暢地** 在 HoloLens 2 裝置上安裝應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-681">We are **adding a new capability (App Installer) to allow you to install applications more seamlessly** on your HoloLens 2 devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-682">**預設會針對未受管理的裝置開啟** 此功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-682">The feature will be **on by default for unmanaged devices**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-683">為了避免對企業造成中斷， **受控裝置** 目前無法使用應用程式安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-683">To prevent disruption to enterprises, app installer will be **not be available for managed devices** at this time.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-684">如果下列 **任一** 條件成立，則會將裝置視為「受控」：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-684">A device is considered “managed” if **any** of the following are true:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-685">已[註冊](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)MDM</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-685">MDM [Enrolled](hololens-enroll-mdm.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-686">已設定布建 [套件](hololens-provisioning.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-686">Configured with [provisioning package](hololens-provisioning.md)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-687">使用者身分 [識別](hololens-identity.md) 為 Azure AD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-687">User [Identity](hololens-identity.md) is Azure AD</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-688">您現在可以安裝應用程式，而不需要啟用開發人員模式或使用裝置入口網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-688">You are now able to install Apps without needing to enable Developer Mode or using Device Portal.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-689">只要將 (透過 USB 或 Edge) Appx 套件組合下載到您的裝置，並流覽至檔案總管中的 Appx 套件組合，系統就會提示您開始安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-689">Simply download (over USB or through Edge) the Appx Bundle to your device and navigate to the Appx Bundle in the File Explorer to be prompted to kick off the installation.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-690">或者， [從網頁起始安裝](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-690">Alternatively, [initiate an install from a web page](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/msix/app-installer/installing-windows10-apps-web).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-691">就像您使用 MDM 的 LOB 應用程式部署功能從 Microsoft Store 或側載安裝的應用程式，應用程式必須使用[簽署工具](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool)進行數位簽署，而[用來簽署的憑證必須](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations)由 HoloLens 裝置信任，才能部署應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-691">Just like apps you install from the Microsoft Store or sideload using MDM’s LOB App deployment capability, apps need to be digitally signed with the [Sign Tool](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool) and the [certificate used to sign must be trusted](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/appxpkg/how-to-sign-a-package-using-signtool#security-considerations) by the HoloLens device before the app can be deployed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-692">**應用程式安裝指示。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-692">**Application install instructions.**</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-693">確定您的裝置未被視為受管理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-693">Ensure that your device is not considered managed</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-694">確定您的 HoloLens 2 裝置已開啟電源並連接到您的電腦</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-694">Ensure that your HoloLens 2 device is powered on and connected to your PC</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-695">確定您已登入 HoloLens 2 裝置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-695">Ensure that you are signed into the HoloLens 2 device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-696">在您的電腦上，流覽至您的自訂應用程式，並將 yourapp 複製到 yourdevicename\Internal 儲存體 \Downloads。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-696">On your PC navigate to your custom app, and copy yourapp.appxbundle to yourdevicename\Internal Storage\Downloads.</span></span>   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-697">複製完檔案之後，您就可以中斷裝置的連線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-697">After you’ve finished copying your file you can disconnect your device</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-698">從您的 HoloLens 2 裝置開啟 [開始] 功能表，選取 [所有應用程式]，然後啟動檔案總管應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-698">From your HoloLens 2 device Open the Start Menu, select All apps and launch the File Explorer app.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-699">流覽至 [下載] 資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-699">Navigate to the Downloads folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-700">您可能需要在應用程式的左側面板上先選取此裝置，然後流覽至 [下載]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-700">You may need to on the left panel of the app select This device first, then navigate to Downloads.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-701">選取 yourapp .appxbundle 檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-701">Select the yourapp.appxbundle file.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-702">將會啟動應用程式安裝程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-702">The App Installer will launch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-703">選取 [安裝] 按鈕以安裝您的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-703">Select the Install button to install your app.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-704">已安裝的應用程式會在安裝完成時自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-704">The installed app will automatically launch upon completion of installation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-705">您可以在[Windows 通用範例 GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples)上找到範例應用程式，以測試此流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-705">You can find sample apps on [Windows Universal Samples GitHub](https://github.com/microsoft/Windows-universal-samples/tree/master/Samples) to test this flow.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-706">瞭解在[應用程式安裝程式 HoloLens 2 上安裝應用程式](app-deploy-app-installer.md)的完整程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-706">Read about the full process of [installing apps on HoloLens 2 with the App Installer](app-deploy-app-installer.md).</span></span>  

![透過應用程式安裝程式安裝 MRTK 範例](images/hololens-app-installer-picture.jpg)

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-708">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-708">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-709">手動追蹤現在可在許多新的情況下持續追蹤，這些案例之前的手將會遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-709">Hand tracking now maintains tracking in many new cases where the hand previously would have been lost.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-710">在這些新的某些情況下，只有掌上的位置會根據使用者的真實手進行更新，而其他接點則是根據先前的姿勢來推斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-710">In some of these new cases, only the palm position continues to update based on the user’s real hand, while the other joints are inferred based on a previous pose.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-711">這項變更有助於改善工匠、擲回、scooping 和鼓掌等移動中的追蹤一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-711">This change helps improve tracking consistency in movements such as slapping, throwing, scooping, and clapping.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-712">如果手接近表面或保存物件，它也會有所説明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-712">It also helps in cases where the hand is close to a surface or holding an object.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-713">當推斷出手接點時， [每個聯合精確度](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) 值會設定為「近似」而不是「高」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-713">When hand joints are being inferred, the [per joint accuracy](https://docs.microsoft.com/uwp/api/windows.perception.people.jointposeaccuracy?view=winrt-19041&preserve-view=true) value will be set to “Approximate” instead of “High.”</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-714">修正 Azure AD 帳戶的 PIN 重設會顯示錯誤「發生錯誤」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-714">Fixed an issue where PIN reset for Azure AD accounts would show an error "Something went wrong.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-715">當啟動 ET、鳶尾花 from settings 應用程式、新使用者或通知快顯時，使用者應該會看到較少的開機後 OOBE 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-715">Users should see much less post-boot OOBE crashes when launching ET, Iris from settings app, new user, or notification toast.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-716">使用者應該有從 OOBE 推出的正確時區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-716">Users should have correct time zone coming out of OOBE.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903--december-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-717">Windows全像版本1903–12月2020更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-717">Windows Holographic, version 1903 – December 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-718">組建18362.1088</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-718">Build 18362.1088</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-719">此每月品質更新不包含任何值得注意的變更，建議您試用最新的 Windows 全像20H2 –2020年12月更新和新的應用程式安裝程式功能新增到組建中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-719">This monthly quality update doesn't contain any notable changes, we encourage you to try out our latest Windows Holographic, version 20H2 – December 2020 Update and the new App Installer feature added in the build.</span></span>


## <a name="windows-holographic-version-20h2"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-720">Windows全像20H2 版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-720">Windows Holographic, version 20H2</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-721">組建19041.1128</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-721">Build 19041.1128</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-722">Windows現已推出全像20H2 版，並為 HoloLens 2 使用者和 IT 專業人員帶來一組絕佳的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-722">Windows Holographic, version 20H2 is now available and brings a great set of new features to HoloLens 2 users and IT professionals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-723">從自動眼睛定位到設定中的憑證管理員，到改良的 Kiosk 模式功能，以及新的 Autopilot 設定功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-723">From Auto Eye Positioning, to Certificate Manager in Settings, to improved Kiosk Mode functionality, and new Autopilot setup capabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-724">這種新的更新可讓 IT 小組更細微地控制 HoloLens 裝置的設定與管理，並提供使用者更流暢的全像攝影體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-724">This new update enables IT teams to take more granular control to configuring and managing HoloLens devices, and offers users even more seamless holographic experiences.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-725">此最新版本是2004版的每月更新，但這次我們會包含新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-725">This latest release is a monthly update to version 2004, but this time we are including new features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-726">主要組建編號會維持不變，Windows Update 將表示2004版 (組建 19041) 的每月版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-726">The major build number will remain the same and Windows Update will indicate a monthly release to version 2004 (build 19041).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-727">您可以在設定 > 有關畫面中查看組建編號，以確認您位於最新的可用組建 19041.1128 +。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-727">You can look at your Build Number in your Settings > About screen to confirm you are on the latest available build 19041.1128+.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-728">若要更新為最新版本，請開啟設定應用程式，移至 [更新 & 安全性]，然後按一下 [檢查更新]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-728">To update to the latest release, open the Settings app, go to Update & Security, and tap Check for Updates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-729">如需有關如何管理 HoloLens 更新的詳細資訊，請造訪[此頁面](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-729">For more information on how to manage HoloLens updates, visit [this page](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-updates).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-eye-position-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-771">自動眼睛位置支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-771">Auto Eye Position Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-772">在 HoloLens 2 中，眼睛可提供精確的全息圖定位、舒適的觀賞體驗，以及改善的顯示器品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-772">In HoloLens 2, eye positions enable accurate hologram positioning, comfortable viewing experience and improved display quality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-773">眼睛的位置會在內部計算為眼睛追蹤計算的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-773">Eye positions are computed internally as part of the eye tracking computation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-774">不過，這會要求每位使用者經過眼睛追蹤校正，即使體驗可能不需要眼睛的輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-774">However, this requires each user to go through eye tracking calibration, even when the experience might not require eye gaze input.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-775">**自動眼睛位置 (AEP)** 可讓這些案例具有無互動的方式，以計算使用者的眼睛位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-775">**Auto Eye Position (AEP)** enables these scenarios with an interaction-free way to compute eye positions for the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-776">自動眼睛位置會從使用者將裝置放置的時刻，自動開始在背景中工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-776">Auto Eye Position starts working in the background automatically from the moment the user puts the device on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-777">如果使用者沒有先前的眼睛追蹤校正，則在處理時間 20-30 秒後，自動眼睛位置將開始提供使用者的眼睛位置給顯示系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-777">If the user does not have a prior eye tracking calibration, Auto Eye Position will start providing the user's eye positions to the display system after a processing time of 20 - 30 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-778">使用者資料不會保存在裝置上，因此，如果使用者關閉並讓裝置重新開機，或裝置重新開機或從睡眠狀態喚醒，則會重複此程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-778">The user data is not persisted on the device and hence this process is repeated if the user takes off and puts the device back on or if the device reboots or wakes up from sleep.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-779">當 uncalibrated 使用者放在裝置上時，會有一些系統行為變更，以及自動眼睛位置功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-779">There are a few system behavior changes with Auto Eye Position feature when an uncalibrated user puts on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-780">在此內容中，uncalibrated 使用者是指尚未在裝置上經歷過眼睛追蹤校正程式的人員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-780">In this context, an uncalibrated user refers to someone who has not gone through the eye tracking calibration process on the device previously.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-781">作用中的應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-781">Active Application</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-782">先前的行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-782">Prior Behavior</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-783">來自 Windows 全像20H2 版更新的行為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-783">Behavior from Windows Holographic, version 20H2 Update</span></span> |
|:-------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-784">未啟用的應用程式或全息式 Shell</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-784">Non-gaze enabled app or Holographic Shell</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="8175b-785">隨即顯示 [眼睛追蹤校正提示] 對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-785">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-786">不會顯示任何提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-786">No prompt is displayed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-787">啟用注視的應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-787">Gaze enabled app</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-788">隨即顯示 [眼睛追蹤校正提示] 對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-788">Eye tracking calibration prompt dialog is displayed.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-789">只有當應用程式存取眼睛眼的串流時，才會顯示眼睛追蹤校正提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-789">Eye tracking calibration prompt is displayed only when the application accesses eye gaze stream.</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-790">如果使用者從未啟用的已啟用應用程式轉換為存取注視資料的應用程式，則會顯示校正提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-790">If the user transitions from a non-gaze enabled application to one that accesses the gaze data, the calibration prompt will be displayed.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-791">所有其他系統行為會類似于目前的使用者沒有使用中的眼睛追蹤校正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-791">All other system behavior will be similar to when the current user does not have an active eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-792">例如，將不會啟用單次開始手勢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-792">For example, the One-handed Start gesture will not be enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-793">初始設定的全新體驗將不會有任何變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-793">There will be no change to the Out-Of-Box-Experience for initial setup.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-794">對於需要眼睛的資料或非常精確的全像全像全像全息的體驗，我們建議 uncalibrated 使用者執行眼睛追蹤校正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-794">For experiences that require eye gaze data or very precise hologram positioning, we recommend uncalibrated users to run eye tracking calibration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-795">您可以從眼睛追蹤校正提示字元進行存取，或從 [開始] 功能表啟動設定應用程式，然後選取 [**系統 > 校正] > 眼睛校正 > 執行眼睛校正**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-795">It is accessible from the eye tracking calibration prompt or by launching the Settings app from the start menu, and then selecting **System > Calibration > Eye Calibration > Run eye calibration**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-796">您稍後可以使用 [其他校正資訊](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support)來找到此資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-796">This information can be found later with [other calibration information](hololens-calibration.md#auto-eye-position-support).</span></span> 

### <a name="certificate-manager"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-797">憑證管理員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-797">Certificate Manager</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-798">透過新的憑證管理員，改進裝置安全性和合規性的審核、診斷和驗證工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-798">Improved auditing, diagnosis, and validation tooling for device security and compliance through the new Certificate Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-799">這項功能可讓您在商業環境中大規模部署、疑難排解及驗證您的憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-799">This capability will enable you to deploy, troubleshoot, and validate your certificates at scale in commercial environments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-800">在 Windows 全息版20H2 中，我們會在 HoloLens 2 設定應用程式中新增憑證管理員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-800">In Windows Holographic version 20H2, we are adding a Certificate Manager in the HoloLens 2 Settings app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-801">移至 **設定 > 更新 & 安全性 > 憑證**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-801">Go to **Settings > Update & Security > Certificates**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-802">這項功能提供簡單且方便使用的方式，可讓您在裝置上查看、安裝及移除憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-802">This feature provides a simple and user-friendly way to view, install and remove certificates on your device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-803">透過新的憑證管理員，系統管理員和使用者現在已改進審核、診斷和驗證工具，以確保裝置保持安全且符合規範。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-803">With the new Certificate Manager, admins and users now have improved auditing, diagnosis and validation tooling to ensure that devices remain secure and compliant.</span></span> 

-   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-804">**審核：** 能夠驗證憑證是否已正確部署，或確認已適當移除憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-804">**Auditing:** Ability to validate that a certificate is deployed correctly or to confirm that it was removed appropriately.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-805">**診斷：** 當問題發生時，驗證裝置上是否有適當的憑證可節省時間，並協助進行疑難排解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-805">**Diagnosis:** When issues arise, validating that the appropriate certificates exist on the device saves time and helps with troubleshooting.</span></span> 
-   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-806">**驗證：** 確認憑證可提供預定用途且正常運作，可節省大量時間，特別是在大規模部署憑證之前的商業環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-806">**Validation:** Verifying that a certificate serves the intended purpose and is functional, can save significant time, particularly in commercial environments before deploying certificates at larger scale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-807">若要快速在清單中尋找特定的憑證，有一些選項可依名稱、儲存或到期日排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-807">To find a specific certificate in the list quickly, there are options to sort by name, store or expiration date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-808">使用者也可以直接搜尋憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-808">Users may also directly search for a certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-809">若要查看個別憑證屬性，請選取憑證，然後按一下 [ **資訊**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-809">To view individual certificate properties, select the certificate and click on **Info**.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-810">憑證安裝目前支援 .cer 和 .crt 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-810">Certificate installation currently supports .cer and .crt files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-811">裝置擁有者可以將憑證安裝在本機電腦和目前的使用者; 所有其他使用者只能安裝到目前的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-811">Device Owners can install certificates in Local Machine and Current User;  all other users can only install into Current User.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-812">使用者只能移除直接從設定 UI 安裝的憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-812">Users can only remove certificates installed directly from the Settings UI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-813">如果已透過其他方式安裝憑證，則也必須使用相同的機制來移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-813">If a certificate has been installed through other means, it must also be removed by the same mechanism.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-install-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-814">若要安裝憑證：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-814">To install a certificate:</span></span> 

1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-815">連線您的 HoloLens 2 到電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-815">Connect your HoloLens 2 to a PC.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-816">將您想要安裝的憑證檔案放在 HoloLens 2 的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-816">Place the certificate file you want to install in a location on your HoloLens 2.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-817">流覽至 **設定應用程式 > 更新 & 安全性 > 憑證**，然後選取 [安裝憑證]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-817">Navigate to **Settings App > Update & Security > Certificates**, and select Install a certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-818">按一下 [匯 **入** 檔案]，並流覽至您儲存憑證的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-818">Click **Import File** and navigate to the location you saved the certificate.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-819">選取 [ **存放區位置**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-819">Select **Store Location**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-820">選取 [ **憑證存放區**]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-820">Select **Certificate Store**.</span></span>
1.  <span data-ttu-id="8175b-821">按一下 [Install] 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-821">Click **Install**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-822">憑證現在應該會安裝在裝置上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-822">The certificate should now be installed on the device.</span></span>

#### <a name="to-remove-a-certificate"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-823">若要移除憑證：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-823">To remove a certificate:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-824">流覽至 **設定應用程式 > 更新和安全性 > 憑證**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-824">Navigate to **Settings App > Update and Security > Certificates**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-825">在搜尋方塊中搜尋憑證（依名稱）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-825">Search for the certificate by name in the search box.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-826">選取憑證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-826">Select the certificate.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-827">按一下 [**移除**]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-827">Click **Remove**</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-828">系統提示您確認時，請選取 [是]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-828">Select **Yes** when prompted for confirmation.</span></span>

![設定應用程式中的憑證檢視器](images/certificate-viewer-device.jpg)

![顯示如何使用憑證 UI 來安裝憑證的圖片](images/certificate-device-install.jpg)

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-831">您可以稍後 [在新的 [憑證管理員] 頁面上](certificate-manager.md)找到此資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-831">This information can be found later [on a new Certificate Manager page](certificate-manager.md).</span></span>

### <a name="auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-832">從 USB 自動啟動布建</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-832">Auto-launch provisioning from USB</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-833">在 OOBE 期間使用具有布建套件的 USB 磁片磁碟機時，可讓使用者互動的自動化程式更少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-833">Automated processes allowing for less user interaction, when USB Drives with Provisioning Packages are used during OOBE.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-834">在此版本之前，使用者必須在 OOBE 期間以手動方式啟動布建畫面，才能使用按鈕組合進行布建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-834">Before this release users had to launch the provisioning screen manually during OOBE to provision using a button combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-835">現在使用者可以使用 USB 存放磁片磁碟機上的布建套件，略過按鈕組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-835">Now users can skip the button combination, by using a Provisioning Package on a USB storage drive.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-836">在 OOBE 的第一個互動時刻插入 USB 磁片磁碟機與布建套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-836">Plug in the USB drive with the provisioning package during OOBE’s first interactable moment</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-837">當裝置準備好要布建時，會自動開啟 [布建] 頁面的提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-837">When the device is ready to be provisioned it will automatically open the prompt with the provisioning page.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-838">注意：如果在裝置開機時，將 USB 磁片磁碟機插入電源，則 OOBE 將會列舉現有的 USB 存放裝置，並監看是否有其他裝置進入電源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-838">Note: If a USB drive is left plugged in while the device is booting then OOBE will enumerate existing USB storage device, as well as watch for additional ones being plugged in.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-839">如需在 OOBE 期間套用布建套件的詳細資訊，請造訪[HoloLens](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup)布建檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-839">For more information about applying provisioning packages during OOBE, visit the [HoloLens provisioning](hololens-provisioning.md#apply-a-provisioning-package-to-hololens-during-setup) documentation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-840">您可以在 HoloLens 布建檔中找到[從 USB 自動啟動布建](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb)的其他資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-840">Additional information on [auto-launch provisioning from a USB](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-launch-provisioning-from-usb) can be found in the HoloLens provisioning documentation.</span></span>

### <a name="auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-841">在 OOBE 中自動確認布建套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-841">Auto-confirm provisioning packages in OOBE</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-842">自動化程式允許較少的使用者互動，當 [布建套件] 頁面顯示時，將會自動套用所有列出的套件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-842">Automated process allowing for less user interaction, when the Provisioning Package page is displayed it will automatically apply all packages listed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-843">當布建主畫面出現時，OOBE 會在自動開始套用所有布建套件之前的10秒內算下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-843">When the provisioning main screen comes up, OOBE will count down 10 seconds before automatically starting applying all provisioning packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-844">使用者仍然可以在確認預期的套件之後，于10秒內 [確認或取消](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-844">Users can still [confirm or cancel](hololens-provisioning.md#auto-confirm-provisioning-packages-in-oobe) within this 10 seconds after verifying the packages they expected.</span></span>

### <a name="automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-845">自動布建而不使用 UI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-845">Automatic provisioning without using UI</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-846">結合自動程式以減少裝置互動以進行布建。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-846">Combined automatic processes for reduced device interactions for provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-847">藉由結合從 USB 裝置自動啟動布建和布建套件的自動確認，使用者可以自動布建 HoloLens 2 裝置，而不需要使用裝置的 UI 或甚至是裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-847">By combining the auto-launch of provisioning from USB devices and the auto-confirmation of provisioning packages, a user can provision HoloLens 2 devices automatically without using the device's UI or even wearing the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-848">您可以繼續針對多個裝置使用相同的 USB 磁片磁碟機和布建套件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-848">You may continue to use the same USB drive and provisioning package for multiple devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-849">這適用于在相同區域中一次部署多個裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-849">This is useful for deploying multiple devices at once in the same area.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-850">使用 Windows 的設定[設計](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22)工具[建立布建套件](hololens-provisioning.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-850">[Create a Provisioning Package](hololens-provisioning.md) using [Windows Configuration Designer](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9NBLGGH4TX22).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-851">將套件複製到 USB 存放磁片磁碟機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-851">Copy the package to a USB storage drive.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-852">將[您的 HoloLens 2 快閃](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions)至[19041.1361 或更新版本的組建](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-852">[Flash your HoloLens 2](hololens-insider.md#ffu-download-and-flash-directions) to [19041.1361 or newer build](https://aka.ms/hololens2previewdownload).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-853">當 [Advanced Recovery 附屬](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) 已完成時，您的裝置就會將 USB-C 纜線拔下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-853">When [Advanced Recovery Companion](https://www.microsoft.com/store/productId/9P74Z35SFRS8) has completed flashing your device unplug your USB-C cable.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-854">將 USB 磁片磁碟機插入裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-854">Plug in your USB drive to the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-855">當 HoloLens 2 裝置開機進入 OOBE 時，它會自動偵測 USB 磁片磁碟機上的布建套件，並啟動 [布建] 頁面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-855">When the HoloLens 2 device boots into OOBE it will automatically detect the provisioning package on the USB drive and launch the provisioning page.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-856">10秒後，裝置會自動套用布建套件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-856">After 10 seconds the device will automatically apply the provisioning package.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-857">現在已設定您的裝置，並會顯示布建 [成功畫面](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-857">Your device is now configured and will [display the Provisioning Successful screen](hololens-provisioning.md#automatic-provisioning-without-using-ui).</span></span>

### <a name="using-autopilot-with-wi-fi-connection"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-858">使用 Autopilot 搭配 Wi-Fi 連接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-858">Using Autopilot with Wi-Fi connection</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-859">藉由讓 Autopilot 可在 Wi-Fi 連線的裝置上運作，讓乙太網路上的 C + + 移除需要減少硬體需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-859">Removed need for USB-C adapters to ethernet reducing hardware needs, by enabling Autopilot to function on Wi-Fi connected devices.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-860">現在在 OOBE 期間，將 HoloLens 2 與 wi-fi 連線之後，OOBE 將檢查裝置的 Autopilot 設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-860">Now during OOBE, once you connect HoloLens 2 with Wi-Fi, OOBE will check for an Autopilot profile for the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-861">如果找到一個，就會用來完成 AAD 聯結和註冊流程的其餘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-861">If one is found it will be used to complete rest of the AAD join and enrollment flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-862">換句話說，使用 ethernet 至 USB-C 或 Wi-Fi 到 USB-C 的介面卡並不是需求，不過如果是在 OOBE 開頭提供，它們仍會繼續運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-862">In other words, using ethernet to USB-C or Wi-Fi to USB-C adapter is not a requirement anymore, however they continue to work if provided at beginning of OOBE.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-863">深入瞭解[HoloLens 2 裝置的 Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-863">Learn more about [Autopilot for HoloLens 2 devices](hololens2-autopilot.md).</span></span>

### <a name="tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-864">Tenantlockdown CSP 和 Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-864">Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-865">透過裝置重設或重新刷新，將裝置鎖定至租使用者，藉此將裝置保持在組織的租使用者上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-865">Keeps devices on the organization's tenant by locking them to the tenant even through device reset or reflash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-866">藉由在中透過布建來禁止帳戶建立，以進一步提供安全性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-866">With further security by disallowing account creation in via provisioning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-867">HoloLens 2 裝置現在支援 Windows 全像[20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2)的 TenantLockdown CSP。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-867">HoloLens 2 devices now support TenantLockdown CSP as of [Windows Holographic version 20H2](hololens-release-notes.md#windows-holographic-version-20h2).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-868">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp)CSP 可讓 HoloLens 2 只能使用 Autopilot 系結至 MDM 註冊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-868">[TenantLockdown](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/tenantlockdown-csp) CSP enables HoloLens 2 to be tied to MDM enrollment using Autopilot only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-869">一旦 TenantLockdown CSP 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 節點設定為 true 或 false (初始在 HoloLens 2 上設定) 值時，即使重新閃爍、OS 更新等，該值仍會保留在裝置上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-869">Once TenantLockdown CSP’s RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to either true or false (initially set) value on HoloLens 2, that value remains on the device despite re-flashing, OS updates, etc.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-870">在 HoloLens 2 上將 TenantLockdown csp 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 節點設為 true 之後，OOBE 會無限期等候 Autopilot 設定檔在網路連線之後成功下載及套用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-870">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, OOBE waits indefinitely for Autopilot profile to be successfully downloaded and applied, after network connectivity.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-871">在 HoloLens 2 上將 TenantLockdown csp 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE 節點設為 true 之後，OOBE 中不允許下列作業：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-871">Once TenantLockdown CSPs’ RequireNetworkInOOBE node is set to true on HoloLens 2, following operations are disallowed in OOBE:</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-872">使用執行時間布建來建立本機使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-872">Creating local user using runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-873">透過執行時間布建來執行 Azure AD 聯結操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-873">Performing Azure AD join operation via runtime provisioning</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-874">選取在 OOBE 體驗中擁有裝置的人員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-874">Selecting who owns the device in OOBE experience</span></span> 

#### <a name="how-to-set-this-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-875">如何使用 Intune 進行設定？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-875">How to set this using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-876">建立自訂 OMA URI 裝置設定檔，並為 RequireNetworkInOOBE 節點指定 true，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-876">Create a custom OMA URI device configuration profile and specify true for RequireNetworkInOOBE node as shown below.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-877">OMA-URI 值應為./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-877">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="8175b-878">![透過 OMA URI 設定租使用者鎖定](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-878">![Setting tennant lockdown via OMA-URI](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-879">建立群組，並將裝置設定檔指派給該裝置群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-879">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-880">將在上一個步驟中建立之群組的 HoloLens 2 裝置成員，並觸發同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-880">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-881">在 Intune 入口網站中確認已成功套用裝置設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-881">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-882">一旦此裝置設定成功套用到 HoloLens 2 裝置上，TenantLockdown 的效果就會是作用中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-882">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be active.</span></span>

#### <a name="how-to-unset-tenantlockdowns-requirenetworkinoobe-on-hololens-2-using-intune"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-883">如何使用 Intune 在 HoloLens 2 上取消設定 TenantLockdown 的 RequireNetworkInOOBE？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-883">How to unset TenantLockdown’s RequireNetworkInOOBE on HoloLens 2 using Intune?</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-884">從先前已指派裝置設定的裝置群組中移除 HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-884">Remove the HoloLens 2 from the device group to which the device configuration created above was previously assigned.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-885">建立自訂 OMA URI 型裝置設定檔，並為 RequireNetworkInOOBE 指定 false，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-885">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration profile and specify false for RequireNetworkInOOBE as shown below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-886">OMA-URI 值應為./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-886">OMA-URI value should be ./Vendor/MSFT/TenantLockdown/RequireNetworkInOOBE</span></span>

   > [!div class="mx-imgBorder"]
   > <span data-ttu-id="8175b-887">![透過 Intune 中的 OMA-URI URI 將 RequireNetworkInOOBE 設定為 false 的螢幕擷取畫面](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-887">![Screenshot of setting RequireNetworkInOOBE to false via OMA URI in Intune](images/hololens-tenant-lockdown-false.png)</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-888">建立群組，並將裝置設定檔指派給該裝置群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-888">Create a group and assign the device configuration profile to that device group.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-889">將在上一個步驟中建立之群組的 HoloLens 2 裝置成員，並觸發同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-889">Make the HoloLens 2 device member of the group created in previous step and trigger sync.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-890">在 Intune 入口網站中確認已成功套用裝置設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-890">Verify in the Intune portal that device configuration has been successfully applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-891">一旦此裝置設定成功套用到 HoloLens 2 裝置上，TenantLockdown 的效果就會變成非使用中狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-891">Once this device configuration successfully applies on the HoloLens 2 device, effects of TenantLockdown will be inactive.</span></span> 

#### <a name="what-would-happen-during-oobe-if-autopilot-profile-is-unassigned-on-a-hololens-after-tenantlockdown-was-set-to-true"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-892">當 TenantLockdown 設定為 true 之後，如果 HoloLens 未指派 Autopilot 設定檔，在 OOBE 期間會發生什麼事？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-892">What would happen during OOBE, if Autopilot profile is unassigned on a HoloLens after TenantLockdown was set to true?</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-893">OOBE 會無限期等待 Autopilot 設定檔的下載，並會顯示下列對話方塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-893">OOBE will wait indefinitely for Autopilot profile to download and following dialog will be presented.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-894">為了移除 TenantLockdown 的影響，裝置必須先使用 Autopilot 向其原始的租使用者註冊，而且 RequireNetworkInOOBE 必須取消設定（如先前步驟所述），才能移除 TenantLockdown CSP 所引進的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-894">In order to remove effects of TenantLockdown, device must be enrolled with its original tenant first using Autopilot only and RequireNetworkInOOBE must be unset as described in previous step before restrictions introduced by TenantLockdown CSP are removed.</span></span> 

![裝置上強制執行原則時的裝置上視圖。](images/hololens-autopilot-lockdown.png)

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-896">您現在可以在 [TENANTLOCKDOWN CSP 和 Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot)下的其餘 Autopilot 中找到這項資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-896">This information can now be found alongside the rest of Autopilot under [Tenantlockdown CSP and Autopilot](hololens2-autopilot.md#tenantlockdown-csp-and-autopilot).</span></span>

### <a name="global-assigned-access--kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-897">全域指派的存取– Kiosk 模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-897">Global Assigned Access – Kiosk Mode</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-898">藉由啟用在系統層級套用 Kiosk 模式的新 Kiosk 方法，來減少 Kiosk 的身分識別管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-898">Reduced Identity management for Kiosk, by enabling new Kiosk method that applies Kiosk mode at the system level.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-899">這項新功能可讓 IT 系統管理員針對多個應用程式 kiosk 模式設定適用于系統層級的 HoloLens 2 裝置，與系統上的任何身分識別沒有任何親和性，並適用于所有登入裝置的人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-899">This new feature allows an IT Admin to configure a HoloLens 2 device for multiple app kiosk mode which is applicable at system level, has no affinity with any identity on the system and applies to everyone who signs into the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-900">深入瞭解這項新功能在[HoloLens 全域指派的存取 kiosk](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md)中的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-900">Read about this new feature in detail in the [HoloLens global assigned access kiosk](hololens-global-assigned-access-kiosk.md).</span></span>

### <a name="automatic-launch-of-an-application-in-multiple-app-kiosk-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-901">以多應用程式 kiosk 模式自動啟動應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-901">Automatic launch of an application in multiple-app kiosk mode</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-902">自動啟動應用程式的專注體驗，進一步增加為 Kiosk 模式體驗選擇的 UI 和應用程式選擇。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-902">Focused experience with automatic app launch, further increasing the UI and app selections chosen for Kiosk mode experiences.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-903">只適用于多個應用程式 kiosk 模式，而只有1個應用程式可以指定為在指派的存取設定中使用下方反白顯示的屬性自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-903">Applies only to multiple-app kiosk mode and only 1 app can be designated to auto-launch using highlighted attribute below in Assigned Access configuration.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-904">當使用者登入時，應用程式會自動啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-904">Application is automatically launched when user signs-in.</span></span> 

```xml
<AllowedApps>                     
    <!--TODO: Add AUMIDs of apps you want to be shown here, e.g. <App AppUserModelId="Microsoft.MicrosoftEdge_8wekyb3d8bbwe!MicrosoftEdge" rs5:AutoLaunch="true"/> --> 
```

### <a name="kiosk-mode-behavior-changes-for-handling-of-failures"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-905">處理失敗的 Kiosk 模式行為變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-905">Kiosk mode behavior changes for handling of failures</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-906">在 Kiosk 模式失敗時排除可用的應用程式，以獲得更安全的 Kiosk 模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-906">More secure Kiosk mode by eliminating available apps on Kiosk mode failures.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-907">稍早遇到套用 kiosk 模式的失敗時，HoloLens 用來在 [開始] 功能表中顯示所有應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-907">Earlier on encountering failures in applying kiosk mode, HoloLens used to show up all applications in start menu.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-908">現在在 Windows 的全像20H2 版中，如果發生失敗，就不會在 [開始] 功能表中顯示任何應用程式，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-908">Now in Windows Holographic version 20H2 in the case of failures no apps will be shown in the start menu as below:</span></span> 

![Kiosk 模式在失敗時的外觀影像。](images/hololens-kiosk-failure-behavior.png )

### <a name="hololens-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-910">HoloLens政策</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-910">HoloLens Policies</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-911">專門針對用來管理裝置的 HoloLens 所建立的裝置管理選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-911">Device management options specifically for HoloLens created for managing the device.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-912">針對 Windows 全像20H2 版的 HoloLens 2 裝置，已建立新的混合現實原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-912">New mixed reality policies have been created for HoloLens 2 devices on Windows Holographic version 20H2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-913">新的可控設定包括：設定亮度、設定音量、停用混合式事實中的錄音記錄、可以收集診斷的設定，以及 AAD 群組成員資格快取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-913">New controllable settings include: setting brightness, setting volume, disabling audio recording in mixed reality captures, setting when diagnostics can be collected, and AAD group membership cache.</span></span>
