| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-926">MixedReality\FallbackDiagnostics</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-926">MixedReality\FallbackDiagnostics</span></span>                   | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-927">控制可收集診斷記錄時的行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-927">Controls behavior of when diagnostic logs can be collected.</span></span>                               | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-928">0已停用，裝置擁有者已啟用1，所有 (預設) 皆已啟用2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-928">0 Disabled, 1 Enabled for Device Owners, 2 Enabled for all (Default)</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-929">MixedReality\HeadTrackingMode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-929">MixedReality\HeadTrackingMode</span></span>                      | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-930">保留供未來使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-930">Reserved for future use.</span></span>                                                                  |                                                                      |
| <span data-ttu-id="8175b-931">MixedReality\AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-931">MixedReality\AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-932">控制將群組成員資格快取用於以 Azure AD 群組為目標的 Kiosk Azure AD 的天數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-932">Controls how many days Azure AD group membership cache is used for Kiosk targeting Azure AD groups.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="8175b-933">請參閱下文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-933">See below.</span></span>                                                           |

### <a name="cache-azure-ad-group-membership-for-offline-kiosk"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-934">離線 Kiosk 的快取 Azure AD 群組成員資格</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-934">Cache Azure AD Group membership for offline Kiosk</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-935">啟用離線 Kiosk 以與 AAD 群組搭配使用，最多可達60天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-935">Enabled Offline Kiosks to be used with AAD groups for up to 60 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-936">此原則可控制將 Azure AD 群組成員資格快取用於指派給已登入使用者 Azure AD 群組之存取設定的天數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-936">This policy controls for how many days, Azure AD group membership cache is allowed to be used for Assigned Access configurations targeting Azure AD groups for signed in user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-937">一旦此原則值設定為大於0的值，則不會使用快取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-937">Once this policy value is set to value greater than 0 only then cache is used otherwise not.</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-938">名稱： AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI 值：./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-938">Name: AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays URI value: ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-939">最小值-0 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-939">Min - 0 days</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-940">最大-60 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-940">Max - 60 days</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-941">正確使用此原則的步驟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-941">Steps to use this policy correctly:</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-942">為以 Azure AD 群組為目標的 kiosk 建立裝置設定檔，並將其指派給 HoloLens 裝置 (s) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-942">Create a device configuration profile for kiosk targeting Azure AD groups and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-943">建立自訂 oma-uri 型裝置設定，將此原則值設定為所需的天數 (> 0) ，並將它指派給 HoloLens 裝置 (s) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-943">Create a custom OMA URI based device configuration which sets this policy value to desired number of days (> 0) and assign it to HoloLens device(s).</span></span> 
    1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-944">URI 值應在 OMA-URI 文字方塊中輸入為./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-944">The URI value should be entered in OMA-URI text box as ./Vendor/MSFT/Policy/Config/MixedReality/AADGroupMembershipCacheValidityInDays</span></span>
    1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-945">此值可介於 [允許的最小/最大值] 之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-945">The value can be between min / max allowed.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-946">註冊 HoloLens 的裝置，並確認兩項設定會套用至裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-946">Enroll HoloLens devices and verify both configurations get applied to the device.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-947">當網際網路可供使用時，讓 Azure AD 使用者1登入，一旦使用者登入和 Azure AD 群組成員資格確認成功，就會建立快取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-947">Let Azure AD user 1 sign-in when internet is available, once user signs-in and Azure AD group membership is confirmed successfully, cache will be created.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-948">現在 Azure AD 使用者1可以讓 HoloLens 離線，並將其用於 kiosk 模式，只要原則值允許 X 天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-948">Now Azure AD user 1 can take HoloLens offline and use it for kiosk mode as long as policy value allows for X number of days.</span></span> 
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-949">您可以針對任何其他 Azure AD 使用者 N，重複執行步驟4和5。此處的重點是任何 Azure AD 使用者都必須使用網際網路登入裝置，至少一次我們可以判斷其是否為 Kiosk 設定目標 Azure AD 群組的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-949">Steps 4 and 5 can be repeated for any other Azure AD user N. Key point here is that any Azure AD user must sign-in to device using Internet so at least once we can determine that they are member of Azure AD group to which Kiosk configuration is targeted.</span></span> 
 
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-950">在針對 Azure AD 使用者執行步驟4之前，會遇到「已中斷連線」環境中提及的失敗行為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-950">Until step 4 is performed for a Azure AD user will experience failure behavior mentioned in “disconnected” environments.</span></span> 

### <a name="new-device-restriction-policies-for-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-951">HoloLens 2 的新裝置限制原則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-951">New device restriction policies for HoloLens 2</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="8175b-954">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-954">AllowAddProvisioningPackage</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-security#security-allowaddprovisioningpackage)

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-958">這兩個 AllowAddProvisioningPackage 和 AllowRemoveProvisioningPackage 的新原則已新增至我們的 [一般裝置限制](hololens-common-device-restrictions.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-958">These two new polices for AllowAddProvisioningPackage and AllowRemoveProvisioningPackage are being added to our [Common Device Restrictions](hololens-common-device-restrictions.md).</span></span>

### <a name="enabled-settings-page-visibility-for-hololens-2"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-991">已啟用 HoloLens 2 的設定頁面可見度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-991">Enabled Settings page visibility for HoloLens 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-993">我們現在已啟用原則，可讓 IT 系統管理員防止系統設定應用程式中的特定頁面可見或無法存取，或針對所有頁面（除了指定的頁面以外）進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-993">We’ve now enabled a policy that allows IT Admins to either prevent specific pages in the System Settings app from being visible or accessible, or to do so for all pages except those specified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-994">若要瞭解如何完全自訂此功能，請按一下下面的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-994">To learn how to fully customize this feature click the link below.</span></span>

### <a name="research-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-998">研究模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-998">Research mode</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-999">在研究模式中，HoloLens 2 會成為電腦視覺研究的強大工具。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-999">While in Research Mode, the HoloLens 2 becomes a potent tool for computer vision research.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1000">相較于先前的版本，HoloLens 2 的研究模式有下列優點：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1000">Compared to previous editions, Research Mode for HoloLens 2 has the following advantages:</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1001">除了 HoloLens (第1代) 研究模式所公開的感應器之外，現在還提供 IMU 的感應器存取權，包括加速計、陀螺儀和磁力計。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1001">In addition to sensors exposed in HoloLens (1st gen) Research Mode, we now provide IMU sensor access including an accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1002">HoloLens 2 提供可與研究模式搭配使用的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1002">HoloLens 2 provides new capabilities that can be used together with Research Mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1003">具體而言，就是存取有向的手勢追蹤和眼睛追蹤 Api，可提供一組更豐富的實驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1003">Specifically, access to articulated hand-tracking and eye-tracking APIs that can deliver a richer set of experiments.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1004">研究人員現在可以選擇在其 HoloLens 裝置上啟用 Research 模式，以存取所有對外的原始影像感應器串流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1004">Researchers now have the option of enabling Research Mode on their HoloLens devices to access all of these external facing raw image sensors streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1005">HoloLens 2 的研究模式也提供加速計、陀螺儀和磁力計讀數的存取權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1005">Research Mode for HoloLens 2 also provides access to the accelerometer, gyroscope, and magnetometer readings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1006">為了保護使用者的隱私權，不會透過研究模式提供未經處理的眼睛追蹤相機影像，但您可以透過現有的 Api 使用眼睛的方向。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1006">To protect users’ privacy, raw eye-tracking camera images are not available through Research Mode, but eye-gaze direction  is available through existing APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1007">請參閱 [研究模式檔](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) 以取得進一步的技術詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1007">Check out the [Research Mode documentation](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/mixed-reality/research-mode) for further technical details.</span></span>

### <a name="recording-length-increased"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1008">錄製長度增加</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1008">Recording length increased</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1009">由於客戶的意見反應，我們增加了 [混合現實捕捉](holographic-photos-and-videos.md)的錄製長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1009">Due to customer feedback we’ve increased the recording length of [mixed reality captures](holographic-photos-and-videos.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1010">依預設，混合現實捕獲將不再受限於5分鐘，但會根據可用的磁碟空間來計算最大錄製長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1010">Mixed reality captures will no longer be limited to 5 minutes by default but instead will calculate the maximum recording length based on available disk space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1011">裝置會根據可用的磁碟空間（最高達80% 的總磁碟空間）來預估錄影最大持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1011">The device will estimate the max video recording duration based on available disk space up to 80% of the total disk space.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1012">如果發生下列其中一種情況，HoloLens 將會使用預設的影片錄製長度 (5 分鐘) ：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1012">The HoloLens will use default video recording length (5 minutes) if one of the following occurs:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1013">預估的記錄持續時間上限小於預設的5分鐘。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1013">The estimated max recording duration is smaller than the default 5 mins.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1014">可用磁碟空間小於總磁碟空間的20%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1014">The available disk space is less than 20% of the total disk space.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1015">您可以在「全像 [照片和](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) 影片」檔中找到完整的需求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1015">You can find the full requirements in our [holographic photos and videos](holographic-photos-and-videos.md#maximum-recording-length) documentation.</span></span> 

### <a name="improvements-and-fixes-in-the-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1016">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1016">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1017">OOBE 中的更多畫面現在處於深色模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1017">More screens in OOBE  are now in dark mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1018">深入瞭解內容應指向線上的最新隱私權聲明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1018">Learn more content should point to the latest Privacy Statement online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1019">解決了使用者無法透過布建套件布建 VPN 設定檔的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1019">Addressed an issue where users could not provision VPN profiles through provisioning packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1020">已修正 VPN 連線的 proxy 設定問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1020">Fixed proxy configuration issue for VPN connection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1021">已更新原則，以停用透過 MDM for NCM for AllowUsbConnection 列舉 USB 函式的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1021">Updated policy to disable enumeration of USB functions through MDM for NCM for AllowUsbConnection.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1022">解決了當裝置設定為[單一應用程式 kiosk](hololens-kiosk.md)時，防止 HoloLens 裝置顯示在檔案總管 over Media Transfer Protocol (MTP) 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1022">Addressed an issue that prevented a HoloLens device from showing up in File Explorer over Media Transfer Protocol (MTP) when the device is set up as a [single-app kiosk](hololens-kiosk.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1023">請注意，在一般情況下，您仍可使用 [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) 原則停用 MTP (和 USB 連線) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1023">Note that MTP (and USB connection in general) can still be disabled using the [AllowUSBConnection](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policy-csp-connectivity#connectivity-allowusbconnection) policy.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1024">修正了 [開始] 功能表中的圖示在 Kiosk 模式中正確調整的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1024">Fixed an issue where icons in the Start menu were scaled correctly in Kiosk mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1025">修正因 HTTP 快取干擾以 Azure AD 群組為目標的 kiosk 模式時發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1025">Fixed an issue due to HTTP caching interfering with kiosk mode targeted to Azure AD groups.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1026">已修正使用者在啟用開發人員模式時，無法使用 [配對] 按鈕的問題，除非他們已停用並重新啟用開發人員模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1026">Fixed an issue where users were unable to use the Pair button after enabling Developer mode with provisioning packages unless they disabled and re-enabled Developer mode.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-2004---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1037">Windows全像版本 2004-2020 年9月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1037">Windows Holographic, version 2004 - September 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1038">組建19041.1117</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1038">Build 19041.1117</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1039">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1039">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1040">解決當 package.appxmanifest 中有 SupportsMultipleInstances = "true" 時，無法在應用程式中偵測 Visual Studio 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1040">Addresses an issue that prevented Visual Studio from debugging an application when SupportsMultipleInstances=”true” is present in the appxmanifest.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1041">此版本包含 NCSI proxy 偵測修正，以解決透過網路 proxy 的網際網路偵測失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1041">This release includes NCSI proxy detection fix to address failed Internet detection over network proxy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1042">NCSI 可以使用電腦 proxy 和每個設定檔 proxy 來偵測網際網路連線能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1042">NCSI can use machine proxy and per-profile proxy for Internet connectivity detection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1043">在未來的版本中，每個使用者的 proxy 將受到 NCSI 的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1043">Per-user proxy will be supported by NCSI in future release.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1044">在大部分的 Windows Mixed Reality 裝置上，當使用者的標頭位於想要前進的中性位置時，向前方向向量會平行至地面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1044">On most Windows Mixed Reality devices, the forward direction vector is parallel to the ground when the user's head is in a neutral position looking forward.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1045">不過，舊版 HoloLens 2 會將向量對齊，而不是相對於顯示面板（相對於理想方向，則會向下傾斜幾度）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1045">However, earlier versions of HoloLens 2 aligned the vector to be perpendicular to the display panels instead, which is tilted downward a few degrees relative to the ideal orientation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1046">較新版本的 HoloLens 2 已更正此情況，以確保各種外型規格的語義一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1046">Newer versions of HoloLens 2 have corrected this to ensure semantic consistency across form factors.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1047">改進了手動追蹤的增強功能，會導致特定案例中的追蹤損失減少。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1047">Improved hand tracking robustness that will result in fewer tracking losses in specific scenarios.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1048">此版本包含改善音訊時間戳記品質的修正程式，可能會對影片捕獲問題造成貢獻。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1048">This release contains a fix to improve audio timestamp quality which may have contributed to video capture issues.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---september-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1049">Windows全像版本 1903-2020 年9月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1049">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - September 2020 Update</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1052">在大部分的 Windows Mixed Reality 裝置上，當使用者的標頭位於想要前進的中性位置時，向前方向向量會平行至地面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1052">On most Windows Mixed Reality devices, the forward direction vector is parallel to the ground when the user's head is in a neutral position looking forward.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1053">不過，舊版 HoloLens 2 會將向量對齊，而不是相對於顯示面板（相對於理想方向，則會向下傾斜幾度）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1053">However, earlier versions of HoloLens 2 aligned the vector to be perpendicular to the display panels instead, which is tilted downward a few degrees relative to the ideal orientation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1054">較新版本的 HoloLens 2 已更正此情況，以確保各種外型規格的語義一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1054">Newer versions of HoloLens 2 have corrected this to ensure semantic consistency across form factors.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---july-2020-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1072">Windows全像 1903-7 2020 月更新版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1072">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - July 2020 Update</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1073">組建18362.1071</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1073">Build 18362.1071</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1074">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1074">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1075">修正了在遺失或再次執行追蹤時，可能導致 Unity 應用程式消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1075">Fixed an issue that could cause holograms to disappear in Unity applications when losing or regaining tracking.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1076">已修正在某些裝置上使用 HoloLens Emulator 搭配硬體加速時，導致獨佔 HoloLens 應用程式損毀 shell 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1076">Fixed an issue that caused exclusive HoloLens apps to crash back to the shell while using the HoloLens Emulator with hardware acceleration on certain devices.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1077">解決有關 HoloLens 2 上的 Windows 裝置入口網站的 HTTPS 轉送問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1077">Addressed an issue concerning HTTPS forwarding for the Windows Device Portal on HoloLens 2.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1088">修正了在混合現實捕獲案例中改善音訊品質的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1088">Fixed a bug to improve audio quality in mixed reality capture scenarios.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1089">具體而言，此修正應該會在 [ **開始** ] 功能表顯示時，消除錄製中的音訊瑕疵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1089">Specifically, this fix should eliminate audio glitching in the recording when the **Start** menu is displayed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1091">已解決問題：當裝置處於待命狀態的狀態為多天之後，混合現實 capture 無法錄製影片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1091">Resolved an issue where mixed reality capture couldn't record video after the device was left in standby state for multiple days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1092">Unity 應用程式的 HolographicSpace UserPresence API 通常是停用的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1092">The HolographicSpace.UserPresence API is generally disabled for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1093">此行為可避免造成某些應用程式在面板翻轉時暫停的問題，即使已啟用 [在背景中執行] 設定亦同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1093">This behavior avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1094">現在已針對 Unity 版本2018.4.18 和更新版本以及2019.3.4 和更新版本啟用 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1094">The API is now enabled for Unity versions 2018.4.18 and later and 2019.3.4 and later.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1095">當您透過 Wi-Fi 連接存取裝置入口網站時，網頁瀏覽器可能會因為憑證無效而無法存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1095">When you access Device Portal over a Wi-Fi connection, a web browser might prevent access to due to an invalid certificate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1096">瀏覽器可能會報告「ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR」之類的錯誤，即使先前已信任裝置憑證也一樣。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1096">The browser might report an error such as "ERR_SSL_PROTOCOL_ERROR," even if the device certificate was previously trusted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1097">在此情況下，您無法進行裝置入口網站，因為沒有忽略安全性警告的選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1097">In this case, you can't progress to Device Portal, as there's no option to ignore security warnings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1098">此更新解決了此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1098">This update resolved the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1099">如果先前已在電腦上下載並信任裝置憑證以移除瀏覽器安全性警告，而且發生 SSL 錯誤，則必須下載並信任新的憑證，才能解決瀏覽器安全性警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1099">If the device certificate was previously downloaded and trusted on a PC to remove browser security warnings, and the SSL error occurs, the new certificate has to be downloaded and trusted to address browser security warnings.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1100">已啟用建立執行時間布建套件的功能，可使用 MSIX 套件來安裝應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1100">Enabled the ability to create a runtime provisioning package that can install an app by using MSIX packages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1101">在 **設定**  >  **系統**  >  **全像投影** 中新增設定，可讓使用者在裝置關機時，自動從混合現實首頁移除所有的全像投影。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1101">Added a setting in **Settings** > **System** > **Holograms** that allows users to automatically remove all holograms from Mixed Reality home when the device shuts down.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1102">修正導致 HoloLens 應用程式變更像素格式以在 HoloLens 模擬器中呈現黑色的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1102">Fixed an issue that caused HoloLens apps that change their pixel format to render black in the HoloLens emulator.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1103">修正在鳶尾花登入期間造成損毀的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1103">Fixed a bug that caused a crash during Iris login.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1104">修正了針對已存在於目前的應用程式重複存放區下載的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1104">Fixed an issue about repeated store downloads for already-current apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1105">修正了錯誤，以防止沉浸式應用程式重複開啟 Microsoft Edge。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1105">Fixed a bug to prevent immersive apps from opening Microsoft Edge repeatedly.</span></span>

### <a name="support-for-windows-autopilot"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1149">支援 Windows Autopilot</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1149">Support for Windows Autopilot</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1150">Windows適用于 HoloLens 2 的 Autopilot 可讓裝置銷售通路預先註冊 HoloLens 至您的 Intune 租使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1150">Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 lets the device sales channel pre-enroll HoloLens into your Intune tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1151">裝置抵達時，即已準備好在您的租使用者下以共用裝置形式進行自我部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1151">When devices arrive, they’re ready to self-deploy as shared devices under your tenant.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1152">若要利用自我部署，裝置必須在安裝程式的第一個畫面中使用 USB-C 到乙太網路連接到網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1152">To take advantage of self-deployment, the device must connect to a network during the first screen in setup by using a USB-C-to-Ethernet.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1153">當使用者啟動 Autopilot 自我部署程式之後，程式會完成下列步驟：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1153">After a user starts the Autopilot self-deploying process, the process completes the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1154">將裝置加入 Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1154">Join the device to Azure Active Directory (Azure AD).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1155">使用 Azure AD，在 Microsoft Intune (或另一個 MDM 服務) 中註冊裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1155">Use Azure AD to enroll the device in Microsoft Intune (or another MDM service).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1156">下載以裝置為目標的原則、憑證和網路設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1156">Download the device-targeted policies, certificates, and networking profiles.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1157">布建裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1157">Provision the device.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1158">向使用者顯示登入畫面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1158">Present the sign-in screen to the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1159">若要深入瞭解[HoloLens 2 評估指南的 Windows Autopilot](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1159">Learn more from the [Windows Autopilot for HoloLens 2 evaluation guide](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-autopilot).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1160">*請洽詢您的帳戶管理員，立即加入 AutoPilot preview。Autopilot 就緒的裝置即將開始寄出。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1160">*Contact your Account Manager to join the AutoPilot preview now. Autopilot-ready devices will begin shipping soon.*</span></span>

### <a name="fido2-security-key-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1161">FIDO2 安全性金鑰支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1161">FIDO2 security key support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1162">有些使用者與公司或學校環境中的其他使用者共用 HoloLens 裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1162">Some users share a HoloLens device with others in a work or school environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1163">因此，使用者不必輸入長的使用者名稱和密碼，就很重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1163">So it's important that users can easily without typing long user names and passwords.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1164">快速身分識別線上 (FIDO) 可讓組織中的任何人 (Azure AD 租使用者) 無需輸入使用者名稱或密碼即可順暢地登入 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1164">Fast Identity Online (FIDO) lets anyone in your organization (Azure AD tenant) seamlessly sign-in to HoloLens without entering a user name or password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1165">FIDO2 安全性金鑰是以標準為基礎的無密碼驗證方法，可採用任何外型規格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1165">FIDO2 security keys are an "unphishable" standards-based passwordless authentication method that can come in any form factor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1166">FIDO 是無密碼 authentication 的開放標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1166">FIDO is an open standard for passwordless authentication.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1167">它可讓使用者和組織在沒有使用者名稱或密碼的情況下登入其資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1167">It allows users and organizations to sign in to their resources without a user name or password.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1168">相反地，他們會使用裝置內建的外部安全性金鑰或平臺金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1168">Instead they use an external security key or a platform key built into a device.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1169">若要開始使用，請參閱 [啟用無密碼安全性金鑰登入](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1169">To get started, see [Enable passwordless security key sign-in](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/authentication/howto-authentication-passwordless-security-key).</span></span>

### <a name="improved-mdm-enrollment-via-provisioning-package"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1170">透過布建套件改進 MDM 註冊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1170">Improved MDM enrollment via provisioning package</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1171">布建封裝可讓您透過設定檔設定 HoloLens 設定，而不是透過 HoloLens 的全新體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1171">Provisioning packages let you set HoloLens configuration through a config file rather than through the HoloLens out-of-box experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1172">先前，布建封裝必須複製到 HoloLens 的內部記憶體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1172">Previously, provisioning packages had to be copied onto the HoloLens internal memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1173">現在可以位於 USB 磁片磁碟機上，以便更容易在多部 HoloLens 裝置上重複使用，而且您可以平行布建裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1173">Now they can be on a USB drive so they're easier to reuse on multiple HoloLens devices and you can provision devices in parallel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1174">布建套件現在也支援在裝置管理中註冊的欄位，因此在布建之後不會進行手動設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1174">Provisioning packages now also support a field to enroll in device management so there's no manual setup after provisioning.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1175">試用此功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1175">To try it out:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1176">從 Windows 存放區，將最新版本的 Windows 設定設計工具下載到您的電腦上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1176">Download the latest version of the Windows Configuration Designer from the Windows store onto your PC.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1177">選取 [布建] **HoloLens 裝置** 布建  >  **HoloLens 2 裝置**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1177">Select **Provision HoloLens Devices** > **Provision HoloLens 2 devices**.</span></span>
2. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1178">建立您的設定設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1178">Build your configuration profile.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1179">然後將建立的所有檔案複製到 USB-C 儲存裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1179">Then copy all files that were created to a USB-C storage device.</span></span>
3. <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1180">將 USB 裝置插入任何最近閃爍的 HoloLens。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1180">Plug the USB-C device into any freshly flashed HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1181">然後按 **下音量** 的  +  **電源** 按鈕，以套用布建套件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1181">Then press the **volume down** + **power** buttons to apply your provisioning package.</span></span>

### <a name="line-of-business-application-install-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1182">企業營運應用程式安裝狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1182">Line-of-business application install status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1183">適用于企業營運應用程式的 MDM 應用程式部署和管理對 HoloLens 來說非常重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1183">MDM app deployment and management for line of business apps is critical to HoloLens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1184">系統管理員和使用者必須查看應用程式安裝狀態，才能進行審核及診斷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1184">Admins and users need to view app install status for auditing and diagnosis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1185">在此版本中，我們已在 **設定** 帳戶中新增更多詳細資料  >    >  。請按一下您的帳戶資訊，以 **存取公司或學校**  >  **帳戶**  >  \*\*\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1185">In this release, we added more details in **Settings** > **Accounts** > **Access work or school** > **Click on your account** > **Info**.</span></span>

### <a name="additional-csps-and-policies"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1186">其他 Csp 和原則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1186">Additional CSPs and policies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1187">設定 [服務提供者 (CSP) ](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) 是一個介面，可讀取、設定、修改或刪除裝置上的配置設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1187">A [configuration service provider (CSP)](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/configuration-service-provider-reference?redirectedfrom=MSDN) is an interface to read, set, modify, or delete configuration settings on a device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1188">在此版本中，我們新增了更多原則的支援，以提高系統管理員部署 HoloLens 裝置的控制權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1188">In this release, we add support for more policies to increase the control administrators have over deployed HoloLens devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1189">如需 HoloLens 所支援的 csp 清單，請參閱[NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1189">For the list of CSPs supported by HoloLens, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1190">此版本新增內容：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1190">New in this release:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1191">**原則 CSP**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1191">**Policy CSP**</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1192">原則設定服務提供者可讓企業在 Windows 裝置上設定原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1192">The Policy configuration service provider enables the enterprise to configure policies on Windows devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1193">在此版本中，我們新增了 HoloLens 的新原則，如下所示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1193">In this release, we added new policies for HoloLens, which are listed here.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1194">若要深入瞭解，請參閱[HoloLens 2 所支援的原則 csp](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1194">To learn more, see [Policy CSPs supported by HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/policies-supported-by-hololens2).</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1195">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1195">LetAppsAccessCamera_ForceAllowTheseApps</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1199">LetAppsAccessGazeInput_ForceAllowTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1199">LetAppsAccessGazeInput_ForceAllowTheseApps</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1200">LetAppsAccessGazeInput_ForceDenyTheseApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1200">LetAppsAccessGazeInput_ForceDenyTheseApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1206">**NetworkQoSPolicy CSP**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1206">**NetworkQoSPolicy CSP**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1207">NetworkQoSPolicy 設定服務提供者會建立網路服務品質 (QoS) 原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1207">The NetworkQoSPolicy configuration service provider creates network quality-of-service (QoS) policies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1208">QoS 原則會根據一組符合的條件在網路流量上執行一組動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1208">A QoS policy performs a set of actions on network traffic based on a set of matching conditions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1209">若要深入瞭解，請參閱 [NETWORKQOSPOLICY CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1209">To learn more, see [NetworkQoSPolicy CSP](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/client-management/mdm/networkqospolicy-csp).</span></span>

### <a name="expanded-usb-ethernet-support-for-5glte-tethered-devices"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1210">5G/LTE 行動網卡裝置的擴充 USB 乙太網路支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1210">Expanded USB Ethernet support for 5G/LTE tethered devices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1211">已新增支援，可讓特定行動寬頻裝置（例如 5G/LTE 電話和 Wi-Fi 熱點）行動網卡至透過 USB 的 HoloLens 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1211">Support was added to enable certain mobile broadband devices, such as 5G/LTE phones and Wi-Fi hotspots, when they're tethered to the HoloLens 2 via USB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1212">這些裝置現在會在 [ **網路設定** ] 中顯示為另一個乙太網路連接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1212">These devices are now displayed in **network settings** as another Ethernet connection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1213">不支援需要外部驅動程式 (行動寬頻裝置。 ) 這項功能會在 Wi-Fi 無法使用且 Wi-Fi 的網際網路連線不夠佳的情況下，啟用高頻寬的連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1213">(Mobile broadband devices that require an external driver aren't supported.) This functionality enables high-bandwidth connections when Wi-Fi is not available and Wi-Fi tethering isn't performant enough.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1214">若要深入瞭解支援的 usb 裝置，請參閱[藍牙和 USB-C 裝置的連線](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1214">To learn more about supported USB devices, see [Connect to Bluetooth and USB-C devices](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-connect-devices).</span></span>  

### <a name="hand-tracking-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1215">手動追蹤改進</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1215">Hand tracking improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1216">此版本包含數個手動追蹤改進：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1216">This release includes several hand tracking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1217">**指標會造成穩定性：** 當掌上 pixels occluded 時，系統現在會 resists 為索引手指進行折讓。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1217">**Pointing pose stability:** The system now resists bending the index finger when it gets occluded by the palm.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1218">當您推送按鈕、類型、捲軸內容和更多功能時，此變更可改善精確度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1218">This change improves the accuracy when you push buttons, type, scroll content, and more!</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1219">**減少意外的空中點擊：** 我們已改善對點擊手勢的偵測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1219">**Reduced accidental air taps:** We improved detection of the air tap gesture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1220">現在許多常見的情況下都有較少的意外啟用，例如當您將手手上的手上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1220">There are now fewer accidental activations in several common scenarios, such as when you drop your hands to your sides.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1221">**使用者交換器可靠性：** 當您共用裝置時，系統現在可以更快且更可靠地更新手邊的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1221">**User switch reliability:** The system is now faster and more reliable at updating the hand size when you share a device.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1222">**減少手竊取：** 我們已改善在感應器上有兩個以上實際操作的案例的處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1222">**Reduced hand stealing:** We improved handling of cases where there are more than two hands in view of the sensors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1223">如果有多人密切合作，則追蹤的手將會從使用者「跳」到場景中的其他人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1223">If multiple people are working close together, there's now a much lower chance that the tracked hand will "jump" from the user to the hand of someone else in the scene.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1224">**系統可靠性：** 修正當裝置處於高負載時，造成手動追蹤停止運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1224">**System reliability:** Fixed an issue that caused hand tracking to stop working when the device is under high load.</span></span>

### <a name="dark-mode"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1225">深色模式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1225">Dark mode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1226">許多 Windows apps 現在都支援深色和淺色模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1226">Many Windows apps now support both dark and light modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1227">HoloLens 2 使用者可以為支援這兩者的應用程式選擇預設模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1227">HoloLens 2 users can choose the default mode for apps that support both.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1228">更新之後，預設的應用程式模式為「深色」，但您可以輕鬆地變更此設定：流覽至 **設定**  >  **系統**  >  **顏色**  >  **選擇您的預設應用程式模式**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1228">After the update, the default app mode is "dark," but you can easily change this setting: Navigate to **Settings** > **System** > **Colors** > **Choose your default app mode**.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1229">這些「內建」應用程式支援深色模式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1229">These "in-box" apps support dark mode:</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1230">設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1230">Settings</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1231">Microsoft Store</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1231">Microsoft Store</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1232">電子郵件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1232">Mail</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1233">Calendar</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1233">Calendar</span></span>

### <a name="system-voice-commands"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1241">系統聲音命令</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1241">System voice commands</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1242">您現在可以在裝置上使用語音命令搭配任何應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1242">You can now use voice commands with any app on the device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1243">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[使用語音操作 HoloLens](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-cortana)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1243">For more information, see [Use your voice to operate HoloLens](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens-cortana).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1244">另請參閱[HoloLens 2 支援的語言](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-language-support)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1244">Also see [Supported languages for HoloLens 2](https://docs.microsoft.com/hololens/hololens2-language-support).</span></span>  

### <a name="cortana-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1245">Cortana 更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1245">Cortana updates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1246">更新後的應用程式會與 Microsoft 365 整合，以協助您在裝置上完成更多工作， (目前僅 US-English) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1246">The updated app integrates with Microsoft 365 to help you get more done across your devices (currently in US-English only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1247">在 HoloLens 2 上，Cortana 不再支援特定裝置特定的命令，例如調整音量或重新開機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1247">On HoloLens 2, Cortana no longer supports certain device-specific commands, like adjusting volume or restarting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1248">新的系統 voice 命令現在支援這些選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1248">These options are now supported by the new system voice commands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1249">深入瞭解我們的[blog](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/)中新的 Cortana 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1249">Learn more about the new Cortana app in our [blog](https://blogs.windows.com/windowsexperience/2020/02/28/cortana-in-the-upcoming-windows-10-release-focused-on-your-productivity-with-enhanced-security-and-privacy/).</span></span>

### <a name="quality-improvements-and-fixes"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1250">品質改進和修正</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1250">Quality improvements and fixes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1251">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1251">Improvements and fixes also in the update:</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1252">引進了使用中的顯示器校正系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1252">Introduced an active display calibration system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1253">這項功能可改善全像影像的穩定性和對齊方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1253">This feature improves the stability and alignment of holograms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1254">它們現在會在您從側邊移到側時保持不變。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1254">They now stay in place when you move your head from side to side.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1255">修正了 Wi-Fi 串流至 HoloLens 會定期中斷的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1255">Fixed a bug where Wi-Fi streaming to HoloLens got disrupted periodically.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1256">如果應用程式指出它需要低延遲的資料流程，請呼叫 [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode 函數](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode)來執行修正。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1256">If an application indicates that it needs low latency streaming, implement the fix by calling the [SetSocketMediaStreamingMode function](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/win32/api/socketapi/nf-socketapi-setsocketmediastreamingmode).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1257">修正在研究模式中串流處理期間發生的裝置停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1257">Fixed a device hang that occurred during streaming in research mode.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1258">修正了錯誤，在某些情況下，當使用者繼續會話時，不會在登入畫面上顯示正確的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1258">Fixed a bug where in some cases the right user wouldn't be displayed on the sign-in screen when resuming a session.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1259">修正使用者無法透過 **設定** 匯出 MDM 記錄檔的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1259">Fixed an issue where users couldn't export MDM logs through **Settings**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1260">修正了緊接在預設設定之後立即追蹤的精確度可能低於預期的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1260">Fixed an issue where the accuracy of eye tracking immediately following out-of-box setup could be lower than expected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1261">修正了在某些情況下，眼睛追蹤子系統無法初始化或執行校正的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1261">Fixed an issue where the eye tracking subsystem failed to initialize or perform calibration under certain conditions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1262">修正了視覺校正會提示使用者已預先校正的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1262">Fixed an issue where eye calibration would be prompted for an already-calibrated user.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1263">修正驅動程式會在眼睛校正期間損毀的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1263">Fixed an issue where a driver would crash during eye calibration.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1264">修正重複電源按鈕按下的問題，可能會導致60秒的系統超時和 shell 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1264">Fixed an issue where repeated power button presses could cause a 60-second system timeout and shell crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1265">改善深度緩衝區的穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1265">Improved stability for depth buffers.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1266">在意見反應中樞中新增 [ **共用** ] 按鈕，讓使用者可以更輕鬆地分享意見反應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1266">Added a **Share** button in the Feedback Hub so users can more easily share feedback.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1267">修正 RoboRaid wan't 正確安裝的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1267">Fixed a bug where RoboRaid wan't installed correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="known-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1268">已知問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1268">Known issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1269">Zh-CN 系統語言的問題可防止語音命令取得混合現實的捕獲或顯示裝置 IP 位址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1269">An issue with the zh-CN system language prevents voice commands from taking a mixed reality capture or displaying the device IP address.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1270">問題需要您在啟動裝置之後啟動 Cortana 應用程式，才能使用 "嗨 Cortana" 語音啟用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1270">An issue requires you to launch the Cortana app after starting the device to use "Hey Cortana" voice activation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1271">如果您已從18362組建更新，您可能也會看到舊版 Cortana 應用程式的第二個應用程式磚，不再適用于 **開始** 使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1271">If you updated from a 18362 build, you may also see a second app tile for the previous version of the Cortana app that no longer works in **Start**.</span></span>

UserPresence API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1306">Temporarily disabled the HolographicSpace.UserPresence API for Unity applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1307">這項變更可避免造成某些應用程式在面板翻轉時暫停的問題，即使已啟用 [在背景中執行] 設定亦同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1307">This change avoids an issue that caused some apps to pause when the visor was flipped up, even if the "run in the background" setting was enabled.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---december-2019-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1315">Windows全像版本 1903-2019 年12月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1315">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - December 2019 Update</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1316">組建18362.1042</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1316">Build 18362.1042</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1317">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1317">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1318">引進了 (LSR) 修正程式的最後一個階段複製。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1318">Introduced last stage reproduction (LSR) fixes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1319">改善的全像影像呈現視覺效果呈現更穩定，並更精確地評估其深度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1319">Improved visual rendering of holograms to appear more stable and crisp by more accurately accounting for their depth.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1320">如果應用程式未正確設定自動安裝的深度，則在這項更新之後，這個徵兆會更明顯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1320">This symptom will be more noticeable after this update if apps don't set the depth of holograms correctly.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1321">修正專屬應用程式的穩定性，以及專屬應用程式之間的流覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1321">Fixed stability of exclusive apps and navigation between exclusive apps.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1322">已解決下列問題：在裝置處於待命狀態的幾天後，混合現實 capture 無法錄製影片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1322">Resolved an issue where mixed reality capture couldn't record video after the device was in standby state for several days.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1323">改良的全像影像穩定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1323">Improved hologram stability.</span></span>

## <a name="windows-holographic-version-1903---november-2019-update"></a><span data-ttu-id="8175b-1324">Windows全像版本 1903-2019 年11月更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1324">Windows Holographic, version 1903 - November 2019 Update</span></span> 
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1325">組建18362.1039</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1325">Build 18362.1039</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8175b-1326">更新中的增強功能和修正：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1326">Improvements and fixes in the update:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1327">修正了在 en CA 和 en-us 初始設定期間， **選取** 語音命令的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1327">Fixed functionality of **Select** voice commands during initial setup for en-CA and en-AU.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1328">改良最新 Unity 和混合現實工具組中遠離最新的視覺物件品質 (MRTK) 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1328">Improved visual quality of objects placed far away in the latest Unity and Mixed Reality Toolkit (MRTK) versions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1329">已修正當 [開始] 功能表開啟然後關閉之前，全像應用程式在啟動時停滯處於暫停狀態的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1329">Fixed addressing issues with holographic applications getting stuck in a paused state on startup until the Start menu was opened and then closed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="8175b-1330">OpenXR HoloLens 2 和模擬器的執行時間一致性修正和增強功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8175b-1330">OpenXR runtime conformance fixes and improvements for HoloLens 2 and the emulator.</span></span>
